--- ViewModels/ItemCreateViewModel.cs ---

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;
using ThriftLoop.Constants;

namespace ThriftLoop.ViewModels;

public class ItemCreateViewModel : IValidatableObject
{
    // ── Core Fields ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    [Required(ErrorMessage = "Title is required.")]
    [StringLength(100, MinimumLength = 3,
        ErrorMessage = "Title must be between 3 and 100 characters.")]
    [Display(Name = "Title")]
    public string Title { get; set; } = string.Empty;

    [Required(ErrorMessage = "Description is required.")]
    [StringLength(1000, MinimumLength = 10,
        ErrorMessage = "Description must be between 10 and 1 000 characters.")]
    [Display(Name = "Description")]
    public string Description { get; set; } = string.Empty;

    [Required(ErrorMessage = "Price is required.")]
    [Range(0.01, 99_999.99, ErrorMessage = "Price must be between ₱0.01 and ₱99,999.99.")]
    [DataType(DataType.Currency)]
    [Display(Name = "Price (₱)")]
    public decimal Price { get; set; }

    [Required(ErrorMessage = "Please select a category.")]
    [StringLength(50)]
    [Display(Name = "Category")]
    public string Category { get; set; } = string.Empty;

    [Required(ErrorMessage = "Please select a condition.")]
    [StringLength(50)]
    [Display(Name = "Condition")]
    public string Condition { get; set; } = string.Empty;

    [StringLength(10)]
    [Display(Name = "Size (optional)")]
    public string? Size { get; set; }

    // ── Images ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    /// <summary>
    /// Up to <see cref="ItemConstants.MaxImagesPerListing"/> images uploaded from the Create form.
    /// Bound from a multiple file input with name="Images".
    /// </summary>
    [Display(Name = "Item Photos (optional)")]
    [DataType(DataType.Upload)]
    public List<IFormFile>? Images { get; set; }

    // ── Stealable Listing Fields ──────────────────────────────────────────────

    [Display(Name = "Make this a Stealable listing")]
    public bool IsStealable { get; set; }

    [Display(Name = "Steal Window")]
    public int? StealDurationHours { get; set; }

    // ── IValidatableObject ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    public IEnumerable<ValidationResult> Validate(ValidationContext validationContext)
    {
        if (IsStealable)
        {
            if (StealDurationHours is null)
            {
                yield return new ValidationResult(
                    "Please select a Steal window duration.",
                    [nameof(StealDurationHours)]);
            }
            else if (!ItemConstants.StealDurations.Contains(StealDurationHours.Value))
            {
                yield return new ValidationResult(
                    $"Steal window must be {string.Join(", ", ItemConstants.StealDurations)} hours.",
                    [nameof(StealDurationHours)]);
            }
        }
    }

    // ── Select-List Options (delegates to constants) ──────────────────────────

    public static IReadOnlyList<string> Categories => ItemConstants.Categories;
    public static IReadOnlyList<string> Conditions => ItemConstants.Conditions;
    public static IReadOnlyList<string> Sizes => ItemConstants.Sizes;
    public static IReadOnlyList<int> StealDurations => ItemConstants.StealDurations;
}

    /// <summary>New images added by the user on the Edit form (name="NewImages").</summary>
    [Display(Name = "Add Photos")]
    [DataType(DataType.Upload)]
    public List<IFormFile>? NewImages { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// The item's current image URLs from the database.
    /// Round-tripped through the form as repeated hidden inputs (name="ExistingImageUrls").
    /// The controller reads this to know which existing images to keep.
    /// </summary>
    public List<string> ExistingImageUrls { get; set; } = new();

    /// <summary>
    /// URLs the user removed in the UI.
    /// Injected by JS as hidden inputs (name="RemovedImageUrls") when a thumbnail × is clicked.
    /// The controller deletes these files from disk and removes them from the DB list.
    /// </summary>
    public List<string> RemovedImageUrls { get; set; } = new();

    // ── Select-List Options (delegates to constants) ──────────────────────────

    public static IReadOnlyList<string> Categories => ItemConstants.Categories;
    public static IReadOnlyList<string> Conditions => ItemConstants.Conditions;
    public static IReadOnlyList<string> Sizes => ItemConstants.Sizes;
}

using ThriftLoop.Enums;
using ThriftLoop.Models;
using ThriftLoop.Constants;

namespace ThriftLoop.ViewModels;

/// <summary>
/// Carries everything the Wallet dashboard view needs: balances,
/// recent transactions, and pending withdrawal requests.
/// </summary>
public class WalletIndexViewModel
{
    // ── Balances ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    public decimal Balance { get; init; }
    public decimal PendingBalance { get; init; }
    public decimal TotalBalance => Balance + PendingBalance;

    // ── History ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    public IReadOnlyList<Transaction> RecentTransactions { get; init; } = [];
    public IReadOnlyList<Withdrawal> Withdrawals { get; init; } = [];

    // ── Context ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    public int CurrentUserId { get; init; }
}

/// <summary>
/// Posted from the Withdraw form.
/// </summary>
public class WithdrawViewModel
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Must be at least <see cref="WalletConstants.MinWithdrawalAmount"/>.
    /// Validated in the controller against the user's live wallet balance.
    /// </summary>
    public decimal Amount { get; set; }

    public WithdrawalMethod Method { get; set; } = WithdrawalMethod.BankTransfer;

    /// <summary>Bank account number or pickup reference.</summary>
    public string? Reference { get; set; }
}

@model ThriftLoop.DTOs.Auth.ForgotPasswordDTO
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Forgot Password";
    ViewData["HideNavbar"] = true;
    Layout = "~/Views/Shared/_Layout.cshtml";
}

<div class="auth-shell">

    <aside class="auth-panel auth-panel--brand">
        <div class="brand-wordmark">ThriftLoop</div>
        <p class="brand-tagline">We'll get you<br>back in no time.</p>
        <div class="brand-decoration" aria-hidden="true">
            <span class="deco-ring deco-ring--lg"></span>
            <span class="deco-ring deco-ring--md"></span>
            <span class="deco-ring deco-ring--sm"></span>
        </div>
    </aside>

    <main class="auth-panel auth-panel--form">
        <div class="form-card">

            <header class="form-card__header">
                <h1 class="form-card__title">Forgot your password?</h1>
                <p class="form-card__subtitle">
                    Enter your email and we'll send you a reset link.
                </p>
            </header>

            @if (!ViewData.ModelState.IsValid)
            {
                <div class="alert alert--error" role="alert">

                </button>

<div class="auth-shell">

                <p class="form-card__subtitle">Sign in to continue to ThriftLoop</p>
            </header>

            @* Google error (e.g. OAuth cancelled) *@
            @if (TempData["ExternalAuthError"] is string extError)
            {
                <div class="alert alert--error" role="alert">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm-.75-4.75a.75.75 0 001.5 0v-4.5a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v4.5zm.75-7a.75.75 0 110 1.5.75.75 0 010-1.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                    <span>@extError</span>
                </div>
            }

            @* Successful password reset redirect *@
            @if (TempData["ResetSuccess"] is string resetMsg)
            {
                <div class="alert alert--success" role="alert">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm3.857-9.809a.75.75 0 00-1.214-.882l-3.483 4.79-1.88-1.88a.75.75 0 10-1.06 1.061l2.5 2.5a.75.75 0 001.137-.089l4-5.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                    <span>@resetMsg</span>
                </div>
            }

            @* Invalid reset link redirect *@
            @if (TempData["ResetError"] is string resetErr)
            {
                <div class="alert alert--error" role="alert">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm-.75-4.75a.75.75 0 001.5 0v-4.5a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v4.5zm.75-7a.75.75 0 110 1.5.75.75 0 010-1.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                    <span>@resetErr</span>
                </div>
            }

            @if (!ViewData.ModelState.IsValid)
            {
                <div class="alert alert--error" role="alert">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm-.75-4.75a.75.75 0 001.5 0v-4.5a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v4.5zm.75-7a.75.75 0 110 1.5.75.75 0 010-1.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                    <div asp-validation-summary="ModelOnly"></div>

            <a asp-action="GoogleLogin" asp-controller="Auth"
               asp-route-returnUrl="@returnUrl"
               class="btn btn--google">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true">

                    <path fill="#34A853" d="M12 23c2.97 0 5.46-.98 7.28-2.66l-3.57-2.77c-.98.66-2.23 1.06-3.71 1.06-2.86 0-5.29-1.93-6.16-4.53H2.18v2.84C3.99 20.53 7.7 23 12 23z" />
                    <path fill="#FBBC05" d="M5.84 14.09c-.22-.66-.35-1.36-.35-2.09s.13-1.43.35-2.09V7.07H2.18C1.43 8.55 1 10.22 1 12s.43 3.45 1.18 4.93l3.66-2.84z" />

                        </button>
                    </div>
                    <span asp-validation-for="Password" class="field__error"></span>
                </div>

                <div class="field field--inline">
                    <label class="checkbox-label">
                        <input asp-for="RememberMe" type="checkbox" class="checkbox-input" />
                        <span class="checkbox-custom"></span>
                        <span class="checkbox-text">Keep me signed in</span>
                    </label>
                </div>

                <button type="submit" class="btn btn--primary">
                    Sign In
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M3 10a.75.75 0 01.75-.75h10.638L10.23 5.29a.75.75 0 111.04-1.08l5.5 5.25a.75.75 0 010 1.08l-5.5 5.25a.75.75 0 11-1.04-1.08l4.158-3.96H3.75A.75.75 0 013 10z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                </button>

                </p>
            </footer>

        </div>
    </main>

</div>

@section Scripts {
    @{
        await Html.RenderPartialAsync("_ValidationScriptsPartial");
    }
    <script>
        function togglePassword() {
            const input = document.getElementById('passwordInput');
            input.type = input.type === 'password' ? 'text' : 'password';
        }
    </script>
}

@section Scripts {
    @{
        await Html.RenderPartialAsync("_ValidationScriptsPartial");
    }
    <script>
        function togglePassword(inputId) {
            const input = document.getElementById(inputId);
            input.type = input.type === 'password' ? 'text' : 'password';
        }

        document.getElementById('passwordInput').addEventListener('input', function () {
            const val  = this.value;
            const fill = document.getElementById('strengthFill');
            let strength = 0;
            if (val.length >= 8)          strength++;
            if (/[A-Z]/.test(val))        strength++;
            if (/[0-9]/.test(val))        strength++;
            if (/[^A-Za-z0-9]/.test(val)) strength++;

            const pct = (strength / 4) * 100;
            fill.style.width = pct + '%';
            fill.className   = 'strength-bar__fill';
            if (strength <= 1)      fill.classList.add('strength-bar__fill--weak');
            else if (strength <= 2) fill.classList.add('strength-bar__fill--fair');
            else if (strength <= 3) fill.classList.add('strength-bar__fill--good');
            else                    fill.classList.add('strength-bar__fill--strong');
        });
    </script>
}

        function togglePassword(inputId) {
            const input = document.getElementById(inputId);
            input.type = input.type === 'password' ? 'text' : 'password';
        }

        document.getElementById('passwordInput').addEventListener('input', function () {
            const val  = this.value;
            const fill = document.getElementById('strengthFill');
            let strength = 0;
            if (val.length >= 8)          strength++;
            if (/[A-Z]/.test(val))        strength++;
            if (/[0-9]/.test(val))        strength++;
            if (/[^A-Za-z0-9]/.test(val)) strength++;

            const pct = (strength / 4) * 100;
            fill.style.width = pct + '%';
            fill.className   = 'strength-bar__fill';
            if (strength <= 1)      fill.classList.add('strength-bar__fill--weak');
            else if (strength <= 2) fill.classList.add('strength-bar__fill--fair');
            else if (strength <= 3) fill.classList.add('strength-bar__fill--good');
            else                    fill.classList.add('strength-bar__fill--strong');
        });
    </script>
}

        }

@section Scripts {
    <style>
        /* ── Stealable badge on card images ─────────────────────────────── */
        .fy-card__stealable-badge {
            position: absolute;
            top: 8px;
            right: 8px;
            display: inline-flex;
            align-items: center;
            gap: 4px;
            background: var(--color-primary, #2d5a27);
            color: #fff;
            font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
            font-size: 0.67rem;
            font-weight: 700;
            letter-spacing: 0.04em;
            padding: 3px 7px;
            border-radius: 5px;
            box-shadow: 0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,.18);
            z-index: 2;
            pointer-events: none;
        }

        .fy-card--sold .fy-card__stealable-badge {
            background: #4b5563;
        }

        /* ── Steal hint text next to price ───────────────────────────── */
        .fy-card__steal-hint {
            font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
            font-size: 0.67rem;
            font-weight: 500;
            color: var(--color-primary, #2d5a27);
            margin-left: 4px;
            vertical-align: middle;
        }

        /* ── Sold card — desaturation ─────────────────────────────── */
        .fy-card--sold {
            opacity: 0.7;
            pointer-events: none;
        }

            .fy-card--sold .fy-card__actions {
                pointer-events: auto;
            }

        /* ── Multi-image cycling ─────────────────────────────────────────── */

        /* The img inside the wrap gets a cross-fade transition */
        .fy-card__img-wrap .fy-card__img {
            transition: opacity 0.25s ease;
        }

            .fy-card__img-wrap .fy-card__img.fy-img--fading {
                opacity: 0;
            }

        /* Progress dots — appear at the bottom of the image on hover */
        .fy-card__dots {
            position: absolute;
            bottom: 8px;
            left: 50%;
            transform: translateX(-50%);
            display: flex;
            gap: 4px;
            z-index: 3;
            opacity: 0;
            transition: opacity 0.2s ease;
            pointer-events: none;
        }

        .fy-card:hover .fy-card__dots {
            opacity: 1;
        }

        .fy-card__dot {
            width: 5px;
            height: 5px;
            border-radius: 50%;
            background: rgba(255,255,255,0.5);
            transition: background 0.2s ease, transform 0.2s ease;
        }

        .fy-card__dot--active {
            background: #fff;
            transform: scale(1.3);
        }

        /* ── Shop item card — subtle purple glow ─────────────────────── */
        .fy-card--shop {
            box-shadow: 0 0 0 1.5px rgba(139, 92, 246, 0.25), 0 2px 8px rgba(139, 92, 246, 0.08);
        }

            .fy-card--shop:hover {
                box-shadow: 0 0 0 2px rgba(139, 92, 246, 0.4), 0 4px 18px rgba(139, 92, 246, 0.15);
            }

        .fy-card__shop-badge {
            position: absolute;
            top: 8px;
            right: 8px;
            background: rgba(139, 92, 246, 0.88);
            color: #fff;
            font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
            font-size: 0.67rem;
            font-weight: 700;
            letter-spacing: 0.05em;
            padding: 3px 7px;
            border-radius: 5px;
            box-shadow: 0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,.15);
            z-index: 2;
            pointer-events: none;
        }

        .fy-card__from-label {
            font-size: 0.75rem;
            font-weight: 400;
            color: var(--color-muted, #8a8278);
            margin-right: 1px;
        }
    </style>

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            // ── Element references ─────────────────────────────────────────────
            var grid         = document.getElementById('itemGrid');
            var filterEmpty  = document.getElementById('filterEmpty');
            var visibleCount = document.getElementById('visibleCount');
            var searchInput  = document.getElementById('searchInput');
            var priceMin     = document.getElementById('priceMin');
            var priceMax     = document.getElementById('priceMax');
            var catChecks    = document.querySelectorAll('#catFilters .fy-check');
            var condChecks   = document.querySelectorAll('#condFilters .fy-check');

            if (!grid) return;

            var cards = Array.prototype.slice.call(grid.querySelectorAll('.fy-card'));

            // ── Multi-image hover cycling ──────────────────────────────────────
            cards.forEach(function (card) {
                var wrap   = card.querySelector('.fy-card__img-wrap');
                var img    = card.querySelector('.fy-card__img');
                var dotsEl = card.querySelector('.fy-card__dots');

                if (!wrap || !img) return;

                var raw = wrap.getAttribute('data-images');
                var images = [];
                try { images = JSON.parse(raw); } catch(e) {}

                // Nothing to cycle if 0 or 1 image
                if (images.length < 2) return;

                var dots     = dotsEl ? Array.prototype.slice.call(dotsEl.querySelectorAll('.fy-card__dot')) : [];
                var current  = 0;
                var timer    = null;
                var INTERVAL = 900; // ms between image switches

                function goTo(idx) {
                    // Cross-fade: fade out → swap src → fade in
                    img.classList.add('fy-img--fading');
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        img.src = images[idx];
                        img.classList.remove('fy-img--fading');
                    }, 220);

                    // Update dots
                    dots.forEach(function (d, i) {
                        d.classList.toggle('fy-card__dot--active', i === idx);
                    });

                    current = idx;
                }

                function startCycle() {
                    if (timer) return;
                    timer = setInterval(function () {
                        var next = (current + 1) % images.length;
                        goTo(next);
                    }, INTERVAL);
                }

                function stopCycle() {
                    if (timer) { clearInterval(timer); timer = null; }
                    // Smoothly reset to first image
                    if (current !== 0) goTo(0);
                }

                card.addEventListener('mouseenter', startCycle);
                card.addEventListener('mouseleave', stopCycle);
                // Touch support: tap cycles forward
                card.addEventListener('touchstart', function (e) {
                    // Only cycle — don't hijack the tap-to-navigate link
                    if (images.length > 1) {
                        var next = (current + 1) % images.length;
                        goTo(next);
                    }
                }, { passive: true });
            });

            // ── Core filter function ───────────────────────────────────────────
            function applyFilters() {
                var query  = searchInput ? searchInput.value.trim().toLowerCase() : '';
                var minVal = priceMin    ? parseFloat(priceMin.value) || 0        : 0;
                var maxVal = priceMax    ? parseFloat(priceMax.value) || Infinity : Infinity;

                var activeCats = [];
                catChecks.forEach(function (cb) { if (cb.checked) activeCats.push(cb.value); });

                var activeConds = [];
                condChecks.forEach(function (cb) { if (cb.checked) activeConds.push(cb.value); });

                var shown = 0;

                cards.forEach(function (card) {
                    var cat   = card.dataset.category;
                    var cond  = card.dataset.condition;
                    var price = parseFloat(card.dataset.price);
                    var title = card.dataset.title || '';
                    var desc  = card.dataset.desc  || '';

                    var catOk   = activeCats.length  === 0 || activeCats.indexOf(cat)   !== -1;
                    var condOk  = activeConds.length === 0 || activeConds.indexOf(cond) !== -1;
                    var priceOk = price >= minVal && price <= maxVal;
                    var textOk  = !query || title.indexOf(query) !== -1 || desc.indexOf(query) !== -1;

                    var visible = catOk && condOk && priceOk && textOk;
                    card.classList.toggle('fy-card--hidden', !visible);
                    if (visible) shown++;
                });

                if (visibleCount) visibleCount.textContent = shown;
                if (filterEmpty)  filterEmpty.classList.toggle('fy-empty--hidden', shown > 0);
            }

            // ── Wire up all controls ───────────────────────────────────────────
            if (searchInput) searchInput.addEventListener('input',  applyFilters);
            if (priceMin)    priceMin.addEventListener('input',     applyFilters);
            if (priceMax)    priceMax.addEventListener('input',     applyFilters);
            catChecks.forEach(function (cb)  { cb.addEventListener('change', applyFilters); });
            condChecks.forEach(function (cb) { cb.addEventListener('change', applyFilters); });

            // ── Reset ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            function resetAll() {
                if (searchInput) searchInput.value = '';
                if (priceMin)    priceMin.value    = priceMin.min  || 0;
                if (priceMax)    priceMax.value    = priceMax.max  || 100000;
                catChecks.forEach(function (cb)  { cb.checked = false; });
                condChecks.forEach(function (cb) { cb.checked = false; });
                applyFilters();
            }

            var resetBtn  = document.getElementById('resetFilters');
            var resetBtn2 = document.getElementById('resetFilters2');
            if (resetBtn)  resetBtn.addEventListener('click',  resetAll);
            if (resetBtn2) resetBtn2.addEventListener('click', resetAll);

            // ── Mobile sidebar toggle ──────────────────────────────────────────
            var toggleBtn = document.getElementById('fyFilterToggle');
            var sidebar   = document.getElementById('fySidebar');
            if (toggleBtn && sidebar) {
                toggleBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    sidebar.classList.toggle('fy-sidebar--open');
                    toggleBtn.setAttribute('aria-expanded',
                        sidebar.classList.contains('fy-sidebar--open').toString());
                });
            }

        }());
    </script>
}

                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm3.857-9.809a.75.75 0 00-1.214-.882l-3.483 4.79-1.88-1.88a.75.75 0 10-1.06 1.061l2.5 2.5a.75.75 0 001.137-.089l4-5.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />

                @successMsg
            </div>
        }

        <!-- Client-side validation error banner (hidden until JS shows it) -->
        <div class="create-error-banner" id="validationBanner" style="display:none">
            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18">
                <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zM8.28 7.22a.75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06L8.94 10l-1.72 1.72a.75.75 0 101.06 1.06L10 11.06l1.72 1.72a.75.75 0 101.06-1.06L11.06 10l1.72-1.72a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06L10 8.94 8.28 7.22z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
            </svg>
            <span id="validationBannerText">Please fix the highlighted fields before posting.</span>
        </div>

        <form asp-action="Create" method="post" enctype="multipart/form-data" id="createForm" novalidate>
            @Html.AntiForgeryToken()

            <div class="create-grid">

                @* ── Photo Column ─────────────────────────────────────────── *@
                <div class="create-photo-col">
                    <p class="create-section-label">
                        Photos <span style="font-weight:400;text-transform:none;letter-spacing:0;font-size:0.6rem">(up to 5)</span>
                    </p>

                    <!-- Thumbnail grid - populated by JS -->
                    <div id="photoThumbs" class="photo-thumbs"></div>

                    <!-- Compact add zone -->
                    <div class="photo-add-zone" id="photoAddZone">
                        <input type="file" id="photosInput" name="Images" multiple
                               accept="image/jpeg,image/png,image/webp" style="display:none" />
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" width="18" height="18" style="opacity:.5">
                            <path d="M3 16.5v-9A1.5 1.5 0 014.5 6h1l1-2h7l1 2h1A1.5 1.5 0 0117 7.5v9A1.5 1.5 0 0115.5 18h-11A1.5 1.5 0 013 16.5z" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                            <circle cx="10" cy="12" r="2.5" stroke-linecap="round" />
                        </svg>
                        <span class="photo-add-zone__cta">Click or drag to add photos</span>
                        <span class="photo-add-zone__hint">JPEG · PNG · max 5 MB each</span>
                    </div>
                    <span class="field__error" id="photoErr"></span>

                    <div class="create-tips">
                        <p class="create-tips__heading">Quick tips</p>
                        <ul class="create-tips__list">
                            <li>First photo is the cover shown on cards</li>
                            <li>Use natural light for best results</li>
                            <li>Show any wear honestly</li>
                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>

                @* ── Form Column ──────────────────────────────────────────── *@
                <div class="create-form-col">

                    @* Title *@
                    <div class="create-field">
                        <div class="create-field__top">
                            <label asp-for="Title" class="create-field__label">Title</label>
                            <span class="create-field__counter" id="titleCounter">0/100</span>
                        </div>
                        <input asp-for="Title" class="create-field__input" id="titleInput"
                               placeholder="e.g. Vintage Levi's 501" maxlength="100" />
                        <span class="field__error" id="titleErr"></span>
                    </div>

                    @* Description *@
                    <div class="create-field">
                        <div class="create-field__top">
                            <label asp-for="Description" class="create-field__label">Description</label>
                            <span class="create-field__counter" id="descCounter">0/1000</span>
                        </div>
                        <textarea asp-for="Description" class="create-field__input create-field__input--textarea"
                                  id="descInput" rows="3" maxlength="1000"
                                  placeholder="Describe the item — colour, fit, any flaws…"></textarea>
                        <span class="field__error" id="descErr"></span>
                    </div>

                    @* Price *@
                    <div class="create-field">
                        <label asp-for="Price" class="create-field__label">Price</label>
                        <div class="create-price-wrap" id="priceWrap">
                            <span class="create-price-wrap__symbol">₱</span>
                            <input asp-for="Price" id="priceInput"
                                   class="create-field__input create-price-wrap__input"
                                   type="number" step="0.01" min="0.01" max="99999.99" placeholder="0.00" />
                        </div>
                        <span class="field__error" id="priceErr"></span>
                    </div>

                    @* Category *@
                    <div class="create-field">
                        <label class="create-field__label">Category</label>
                        <select asp-for="Category" class="create-hidden-select" id="categorySelect">
                            <option value=""></option>
                            @foreach (var cat in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemCreateViewModel.Categories)
                            {
                                <option value="@cat">@cat</option>
                            }
                        </select>
                        <div class="create-chips" id="categoryChips">
                            @foreach (var cat in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemCreateViewModel.Categories)
                            {
                                <button type="button" class="create-chip @(Model.Category == cat ? "create-chip--active" : "")"
                                        data-value="@cat" data-target="categorySelect">
                                    @cat
                                </button>
                            }
                        </div>
                        <span class="field__error" id="categoryErr"></span>
                    </div>

                    @* Condition *@
                    <div class="create-field">
                        <label class="create-field__label">Condition</label>
                        <select asp-for="Condition" class="create-hidden-select" id="conditionSelect">
                            <option value=""></option>
                            @foreach (var cond in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemCreateViewModel.Conditions)
                            {
                                <option value="@cond">@cond</option>
                            }
                        </select>
                        <div class="create-condition" id="conditionPills">
                            @{
                                var icons = new[] { "✦", "★", "◆", "▲", "●" };
                                var idx = 0;
                            }
                            @foreach (var cond in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemCreateViewModel.Conditions)
                            {
                                <button type="button"
                                        class="create-condition__pill @(Model.Condition == cond ? "create-condition__pill--active" : "")"
                                        data-value="@cond" data-target="conditionSelect">
                                    <span>@icons[idx]</span> <span>@cond</span>
                                </button>
                                idx++;
                            }
                        </div>
                        <span class="field__error" id="conditionErr"></span>
                    </div>

                    @* Size — optional *@
                    <div class="create-field">
                        <div class="create-field__top">
                            <label class="create-field__label">Size</label>
                            <span class="create-field__optional">optional</span>
                        </div>
                        <select asp-for="Size" class="create-hidden-select" id="sizeSelect">
                            <option value=""></option>
                            @foreach (var size in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemCreateViewModel.Sizes)
                            {
                                <option value="@size">@size</option>
                            }
                        </select>
                        <div class="create-chips" id="sizeChips">
                            @foreach (var size in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemCreateViewModel.Sizes)
                            {
                                <button type="button"
                                        class="create-chip @(Model.Size == size ? "create-chip--active" : "")"
                                        data-value="@size" data-target="sizeSelect">
                                    @size
                                </button>
                            }
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    @* ── Stealable Listing Section ─────────────────────────── *@
                    <div class="create-field create-field--stealable">
                        <div class="create-stealable-header">
                            <div>
                                <p class="create-field__label">Listing Type</p>
                                <p class="create-stealable-header__sub">
                                    Stealable listings let buyers compete — one claims it, another can steal it.
                                </p>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <label class="stealable-toggle" for="IsStealable">
                            <span class="stealable-toggle__track">
                                <input asp-for="IsStealable" id="IsStealable" type="checkbox"
                                       class="stealable-toggle__input" />
                                <span class="stealable-toggle__thumb" aria-hidden="true"></span>
                            </span>
                            <span class="stealable-toggle__label-group">
                                <span class="stealable-toggle__name">Make this a Stealable listing</span>
                                <span class="stealable-toggle__badge" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="11" height="11">
                                        <path d="M8.75 3.75a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v3.5h-3.5a.75.75 0 000 1.5h3.5v3.5a.75.75 0 001.5 0v-3.5h3.5a.75.75 0 000-1.5h-3.5v-3.5z" />
                                    </svg>
                                    NEW
                                </span>
                            </span>
                        </label>

                        <div class="stealable-duration-panel" id="stealDurationPanel"
                             @(Model.IsStealable ? "" : "hidden") aria-live="polite">
                            <div class="stealable-duration-inner">
                                <svg class="stealable-duration-icon" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18">
                                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm.75-13a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v5c0 .414.336.75.75.75h4a.75.75 0 000-1.5h-3.25V5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                </svg>
                                <div class="stealable-duration-body">
                                    <label asp-for="StealDurationHours" class="create-field__label">Steal Window Duration</label>
                                    <p class="stealable-duration-body__hint">
                                        How long a buyer has before another can steal the item.
                                        After the window closes, the original buyer gets a 2-hour grace period.
                                    </p>
                                    <select asp-for="StealDurationHours" class="create-hidden-select" id="stealDurationSelect">
                                        <option value=""></option>
                                        @foreach (var hours in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemCreateViewModel.StealDurations)
                                        {
                                            <option value="@hours">@hours hours</option>
                                        }
                                    </select>
                                    <div class="create-chips" id="durationChips">
                                        @foreach (var hours in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemCreateViewModel.StealDurations)
                                        {
                                            <button type="button"
                                                    class="create-chip @(Model.StealDurationHours == hours ? "create-chip--active" : "")"
                                                    data-value="@hours" data-target="stealDurationSelect">
                                                @hours hr
                                            </button>
                                        }
                                    </div>
                                    <span class="field__error" id="durationErr"></span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    @* Actions *@
                    <div class="create-actions">
                        <button type="submit" class="btn btn--primary" id="submitBtn">
                            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor">
                                <path d="M10 1a9 9 0 100 18A9 9 0 0010 1zm4.53 6.03l-5 5a.75.75 0 01-1.06 0l-2-2a.75.75 0 111.06-1.06l1.47 1.47 4.47-4.47a.75.75 0 111.06 1.06z" />
                            </svg>
                            Post Listing
                        </button>
                        <a asp-action="Index" asp-controller="Home" class="btn btn--ghost">Cancel</a>
                    </div>

                </div>
            </div>
        </form>
    </div>
</div>

@section Scripts {
    @{
        await Html.RenderPartialAsync("_ValidationScriptsPartial");
    }

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var MAX_PHOTOS = 5;
            var fileList   = new DataTransfer(); // virtual file list maintained by JS

            // ── DOM refs ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            var addZone    = document.getElementById('photoAddZone');
            var photosInput = document.getElementById('photosInput');
            var thumbsEl   = document.getElementById('photoThumbs');
            var photoErr   = document.getElementById('photoErr');
            var form       = document.getElementById('createForm');
            var submitBtn  = document.getElementById('submitBtn');
            var banner     = document.getElementById('validationBanner');
            var bannerText = document.getElementById('validationBannerText');

            // ── Photo: add zone click / drag ──────────────────────────────────────
            addZone.addEventListener('click', function () { photosInput.click(); });

            addZone.addEventListener('dragover', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                addZone.classList.add('photo-add-zone--drag');
            });
            addZone.addEventListener('dragleave', function () {
                addZone.classList.remove('photo-add-zone--drag');
            });
            addZone.addEventListener('drop', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                addZone.classList.remove('photo-add-zone--drag');
                addFiles(Array.from(e.dataTransfer.files));
            });

            photosInput.addEventListener('change', function () {
                var selectedFiles = Array.from(photosInput.files); // capture BEFORE clearing
                photosInput.value = '';                            // reset native picker
                addFiles(selectedFiles);                           // syncInput runs last → files stay
            });

            function addFiles(files) {
                var errors = [];
                for (var i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
                    if (fileList.files.length >= MAX_PHOTOS) break;
                    var f = files[i];
                    if (!['image/jpeg','image/png','image/webp'].includes(f.type)) {
                        errors.push('Only JPEG, PNG, or WebP images are accepted.');
                        continue;
                    }
                    if (f.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) {
                        errors.push(f.name + ' exceeds 5 MB.');
                        continue;
                    }
                    fileList.items.add(f);
                }
                if (errors.length) photoErr.textContent = errors[0];
                syncInput();
                renderThumbs();
            }

            function removeFile(idx) {
                var newDt = new DataTransfer();
                Array.from(fileList.files).forEach(function (f, i) {
                    if (i !== idx) newDt.items.add(f);
                });
                fileList = newDt;
                syncInput();
                renderThumbs();
            }

            function syncInput() {
                photosInput.files = fileList.files;
            }

            function renderThumbs() {
                thumbsEl.innerHTML = '';
                var files = Array.from(fileList.files);
                files.forEach(function (file, i) {
                    var div = document.createElement('div');
                    div.className = 'photo-thumb';

                    var img = document.createElement('img');
                    img.alt = 'Photo ' + (i + 1);
                    var reader = new FileReader();
                    reader.onload = function (e) { img.src = e.target.result; };
                    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
                    div.appendChild(img);

                    if (i === 0) {
                        var badge = document.createElement('span');
                        badge.className = 'photo-thumb__badge';
                        badge.textContent = 'Cover';
                        div.appendChild(badge);
                    }

                    var rm = document.createElement('button');
                    rm.type = 'button';
                    rm.className = 'photo-thumb__remove';
                    rm.innerHTML = '×';
                    rm.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Remove photo');
                    (function (idx) {
                        rm.addEventListener('click', function () { removeFile(idx); });
                    }(i));
                    div.appendChild(rm);

                    thumbsEl.appendChild(div);
                });

                // Show/hide add zone
                if (files.length >= MAX_PHOTOS) {
                    addZone.classList.add('photo-add-zone--hidden');
                } else {
                    addZone.classList.remove('photo-add-zone--hidden');
                }

                // Clear photo error when thumbs are present
                if (files.length > 0) photoErr.textContent = '';
            }

            // ── Character counters ────────────────────────────────────────────────
            function initCounter(inputId, counterId, max) {
                var input   = document.getElementById(inputId);
                var counter = document.getElementById(counterId);
                if (!input || !counter) return;
                var update = function () {
                    var len = input.value.length;
                    counter.textContent = len + '/' + max;
                    counter.classList.toggle('create-field__counter--warn', len > max * 0.9);
                };
                input.addEventListener('input', update);
                update();
            }
            initCounter('titleInput', 'titleCounter', 100);
            initCounter('descInput',  'descCounter',  1000);

            // ── Required chips (category, condition) ──────────────────────────────
            function initChips(containerId) {
                var container = document.getElementById(containerId);
                if (!container) return;
                container.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    var btn = e.target.closest('[data-value]');
                    if (!btn) return;
                    var select = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
                    if (!select) return;
                    container.querySelectorAll('[data-value]').forEach(function (b) {
                        b.classList.remove('create-chip--active','create-condition__pill--active');
                    });
                    btn.classList.add(containerId === 'categoryChips' ? 'create-chip--active' : 'create-condition__pill--active');
                    select.value = btn.dataset.value;
                    // Clear the error for this field
                    var errId = containerId === 'categoryChips' ? 'categoryErr' : 'conditionErr';
                    var errEl = document.getElementById(errId);
                    if (errEl) errEl.textContent = '';
                    container.classList.remove('chips-error');
                });
            }
            initChips('categoryChips');
            initChips('conditionPills');

            // ── Optional chips (size) — second click deselects ────────────────────
            (function () {
                var container = document.getElementById('sizeChips');
                var select    = document.getElementById('sizeSelect');
                if (!container || !select) return;
                container.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    var btn = e.target.closest('[data-value]');
                    if (!btn) return;
                    var already = btn.classList.contains('create-chip--active');
                    container.querySelectorAll('[data-value]').forEach(function (b) {
                        b.classList.remove('create-chip--active');
                    });
                    if (already) { select.value = ''; }
                    else { btn.classList.add('create-chip--active'); select.value = btn.dataset.value; }
                });
            }());

            // ── Duration chips ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            (function () {
                var container = document.getElementById('durationChips');
                var select    = document.getElementById('stealDurationSelect');
                if (!container || !select) return;
                container.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    var btn = e.target.closest('[data-value]');
                    if (!btn) return;
                    container.querySelectorAll('[data-value]').forEach(function (b) {
                        b.classList.remove('create-chip--active');
                    });
                    btn.classList.add('create-chip--active');
                    select.value = btn.dataset.value;
                    var errEl = document.getElementById('durationErr');
                    if (errEl) errEl.textContent = '';
                    container.classList.remove('chips-error');
                });
            }());

            // ── Stealable toggle ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
            (function () {
                var checkbox = document.getElementById('IsStealable');
                var panel    = document.getElementById('stealDurationPanel');
                var durSel   = document.getElementById('stealDurationSelect');
                if (!checkbox || !panel) return;
                function sync() {
                    if (checkbox.checked) {
                        panel.removeAttribute('hidden');
                    } else {
                        panel.setAttribute('hidden', '');
                        if (durSel) { durSel.value = ''; }
                        document.querySelectorAll('#durationChips [data-value]').forEach(function (b) {
                            b.classList.remove('create-chip--active');
                        });
                    }
                }
                checkbox.addEventListener('change', sync);
                sync();
            }());

            // ── Auto-clear input errors on change ────────────────────────────────
            function bindClearError(inputId, errId, wrapId) {
                var el = document.getElementById(inputId);
                if (!el) return;
                el.addEventListener('input', function () {
                    el.classList.remove('input-error');
                    if (wrapId) document.getElementById(wrapId) && document.getElementById(wrapId).classList.remove('input-error');
                    var errEl = document.getElementById(errId);
                    if (errEl) errEl.textContent = '';
                    if (banner.style.display !== 'none') {
                        // Re-check if any errors remain
                        var anyErr = document.querySelectorAll('.input-error, .chips-error, .field__error:not(:empty)').length;
                        if (!anyErr) banner.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                });
            }
            bindClearError('titleInput', 'titleErr');
            bindClearError('descInput',  'descErr');
            bindClearError('priceInput', 'priceErr', 'priceWrap');

            // ── Client-side form validation ───────────────────────────────────────
            function showErr(errId, msg) {
                var el = document.getElementById(errId);
                if (el) el.textContent = msg;
            }
            function markInputErr(inputId, wrapId) {
                var el = document.getElementById(inputId);
                if (el) el.classList.add('input-error');
                if (wrapId) { var w = document.getElementById(wrapId); if (w) w.classList.add('input-error'); }
                return el;
            }
            function markChipsErr(containerId) {
                var el = document.getElementById(containerId);
                if (el) el.classList.add('chips-error');
                return el;
            }

            function validate() {
                var firstErrEl = null;
                var ok = true;

                // Clear previous
                ['titleErr','descErr','priceErr','categoryErr','conditionErr','durationErr','photoErr'].forEach(function (id) {
                    var el = document.getElementById(id); if (el) el.textContent = '';
                });
                document.querySelectorAll('.input-error').forEach(function (el) { el.classList.remove('input-error'); });
                document.querySelectorAll('.chips-error').forEach(function (el) { el.classList.remove('chips-error'); });

                // Title
                var titleEl = document.getElementById('titleInput');
                var titleLen = titleEl ? titleEl.value.trim().length : 0;
                if (titleLen < 3 || titleLen > 100) {
                    showErr('titleErr', 'Title must be between 3 and 100 characters.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markInputErr('titleInput');
                    ok = false;
                }

                // Description
                var descEl = document.getElementById('descInput');
                var descLen = descEl ? descEl.value.trim().length : 0;
                if (descLen < 10 || descLen > 1000) {
                    showErr('descErr', 'Description must be between 10 and 1 000 characters.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markInputErr('descInput');
                    ok = false;
                }

                // Price
                var priceEl = document.getElementById('priceInput');
                var priceVal = priceEl ? parseFloat(priceEl.value) : NaN;
                if (!priceEl || !priceEl.value || isNaN(priceVal) || priceVal < 0.01 || priceVal > 99999.99) {
                    showErr('priceErr', 'Price must be between ₱0.01 and ₱99,999.99.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markInputErr('priceInput', 'priceWrap');
                    ok = false;
                }

                // Category
                var catSel = document.getElementById('categorySelect');
                if (!catSel || !catSel.value) {
                    showErr('categoryErr', 'Please select a category.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markChipsErr('categoryChips');
                    ok = false;
                }

                // Condition
                var condSel = document.getElementById('conditionSelect');
                if (!condSel || !condSel.value) {
                    showErr('conditionErr', 'Please select a condition.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markChipsErr('conditionPills');
                    ok = false;
                }

                // Steal duration
                var stealChk = document.getElementById('IsStealable');
                if (stealChk && stealChk.checked) {
                    var durSel = document.getElementById('stealDurationSelect');
                    if (!durSel || !durSel.value) {
                        showErr('durationErr', 'Please select a Steal window duration.');
                        firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markChipsErr('durationChips');
                        ok = false;
                    }
                }

                if (!ok) {
                    banner.style.display = 'flex';
                    if (firstErrEl) firstErrEl.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                } else {
                    banner.style.display = 'none';
                }

                return ok;
            }

            // ── Submit handler ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            form.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault(); // Always prevent — let our validate() decide
                if (!validate()) return;
                submitBtn.disabled = true;
                submitBtn.innerHTML = '<svg class="spin" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path d="M10 3a7 7 0 100 14A7 7 0 0010 3z" opacity=".25"/></svg> Posting…';
                form.submit(); // Programmatic submit bypasses event listeners
            });

            // ── Auto-dismiss toast ────────────────────────────────────────────────
            var toast = document.querySelector('.create-toast');
            if (toast) {
                setTimeout(function () {
                    toast.style.opacity = '0';
                    setTimeout(function () { toast.remove(); }, 400);
                }, 4000);
            }

        }());
    </script>
}

--- Views/Items/Delete.cshtml ---

@model ThriftLoop.Models.Item
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Delete Listing";
}

<div class="container">
    <div class="confirm-shell">
        <div class="confirm-card">

            <div class="confirm-card__icon">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5">
                    <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M12 9v3.75m-9.303 3.376c-.866 1.5.217 3.374 1.948 3.374h14.71c1.73 0 2.813-1.874 1.948-3.374L13.949 3.378c-.866-1.5-3.032-1.5-3.898 0L2.697 16.126zM12 15.75h.007v.008H12v-.008z" />
                </svg>
            </div>

            <h1 class="confirm-card__title">Delete this listing?</h1>
            <p class="confirm-card__body">
                This action is permanent and cannot be undone.
            </p>

            <div class="confirm-item">
                @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(Model.ImageUrl))
                {
                    <img src="@Model.ImageUrl" alt="@Model.Title" class="confirm-item__img" />
                }
                else
                {
                    <div class="confirm-item__img confirm-item__img--placeholder">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor">
                            <rect x="3" y="3" width="18" height="18" rx="3" />
                            <circle cx="8.5" cy="8.5" r="1.5" />
                            <path d="M21 15l-5-5L5 21" />
                        </svg>
                    </div>
                }
                <div>
                    <p class="confirm-item__title">@Model.Title</p>
                    <p class="confirm-item__price">₱@Model.Price.ToString("N2")</p>
                </div>
            </div>

            <div class="confirm-actions">
                <a asp-action="Index" class="btn btn--ghost">Cancel</a>
                <form asp-action="Delete" asp-route-id="@Model.Id" method="post" id="deleteForm">
                    @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                    <button type="submit" class="btn btn--danger" id="deleteBtn">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.75 1A2.75 2.75 0 006 3.75v.443c-.795.077-1.584.176-2.365.298a.75.75 0 10.23 1.482l.149-.022.841 10.518A2.75 2.75 0 007.596 19h4.807a2.75 2.75 0 002.742-2.53l.841-10.52.149.023a.75.75 0 00.23-1.482A41.03 41.03 0 0014 4.193V3.75A2.75 2.75 0 0011.25 1h-2.5zM10 4c.84 0 1.673.025 2.5.075V3.75c0-.69-.56-1.25-1.25-1.25h-2.5c-.69 0-1.25.56-1.25 1.25v.325C8.327 4.025 9.16 4 10 4zM8.58 7.72a.75.75 0 00-1.5.06l.3 7.5a.75.75 0 101.5-.06l-.3-7.5zm4.34.06a.75.75 0 10-1.5-.06l-.3 7.5a.75.75 0 101.5.06l.3-7.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        Yes, Delete
                    </button>
                </form>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        document.getElementById('deleteForm')?.addEventListener('submit', function() {
            const btn = document.getElementById('deleteBtn');
            btn.disabled = true;
            btn.textContent = 'Deleting...';
        });
    </script>
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;

        }

--- Views/Items/Details.cshtml ---

@model ThriftLoop.Models.Item
@using ThriftLoop.Models
@using ThriftLoop.Enums
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = Model.Title;
    Layout = "~/Views/Shared/_Layout.cshtml";

    bool isOwner = (bool)(ViewBag.IsOwner ?? false);
    bool isAnonymous = (bool)(ViewBag.IsAnonymous ?? true);
    bool isCurrentWinner = (bool)(ViewBag.IsCurrentWinner ?? false);
    bool isOriginalGetter = (bool)(ViewBag.IsOriginalGetter ?? false);

    bool isStealable = Model.ListingType == ListingType.Stealable;
    bool stealWindowOpen = isStealable
                           && Model.Status == ItemStatus.Reserved
                           && Model.StealEndsAt.HasValue
                           && DateTime.UtcNow <= Model.StealEndsAt.Value;

    string sellerDisplay = Model.User is not null
        ? Model.User.Email.Split('@')[0]
        : "Unknown seller";

    string condClass = Model.Condition switch
    {
        "New" => "detail-condition--new",
        "Like New" => "detail-condition--like-new",
        "Good" => "detail-condition--good",
        "Fair" => "detail-condition--fair",
        _ => "detail-condition--poor"
    };

    string priceLabel = isStealable ? "Starting price" : "Fixed price";
    if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.Reserved)
        priceLabel = "Current price";
    if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.StolenPendingCheckout)
        priceLabel = "Stolen price";

    bool hasImages = Model.ImageUrls.Count > 0;
}

                    @if (isStealable)

                            </svg>
                            Stealable
                        </span>
                    }
                </div>

                @if (Model.ImageUrls.Count > 1)
                {
                    <div class="gallery-thumbs" id="galleryThumbs" role="list">
                        @for (int t = 0; t < Model.ImageUrls.Count; t++)
                        {
                            <button type="button"
                                    class="gallery-thumb @(t == 0 ? "gallery-thumb--active" : "")"
                                    data-index="@t"
                                    data-src="@Model.ImageUrls[t]"
                                    role="listitem"
                                    aria-label="Photo @(t + 1)">
                                <img src="@Model.ImageUrls[t]" alt="Thumbnail @(t + 1)" loading="lazy" />
                                @if (t == 0)
                                {
                                    <span class="gallery-thumb__cover">Cover</span>
                                }
                            </button>
                        }
                    </div>
                }

            </div>

            @* Seller card *@
            <div class="detail-seller detail-seller--below-img">
                <div class="detail-seller__avatar" aria-hidden="true">
                    @sellerDisplay.Substring(0, 1).ToUpper()
                </div>
                <div class="detail-seller__info">
                    <p class="detail-seller__label">Listed by</p>
                    <p class="detail-seller__name">@sellerDisplay</p>
                    <p class="detail-seller__since">
                        Member since @(Model.User?.CreatedAt.ToString("MMMM yyyy") ?? "—")
                    </p>
                </div>
            </div>

        </aside>

        @* ════════════════════════════════
           RIGHT — Details
           ════════════════════════════════ *@
        <section class="detail-info-col">

            <div class="detail-meta-row">
                <span class="detail-category">@Model.Category</span>
                <span class="detail-condition @condClass">@Model.Condition</span>
                @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(Model.Size))
                {
                    <span class="detail-size">@Model.Size</span>
                }
                @if (isStealable)
                {
                    <span class="detail-listing-type-badge">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" fill="currentColor" width="10" height="10" aria-hidden="true">
                            <path d="M7 1a6 6 0 100 12A6 6 0 007 1zm.6 8.9H6.4V6.4h1.2v3.5zm0-4.6H6.4V4.1h1.2v1.2z" />
                        </svg>
                        Stealable
                    </span>
                }
            </div>

            <h1 class="detail-title">@Model.Title</h1>

            <div class="detail-price-block">

                            </svg>

                            </p>

                    </div>

                else if (Model.IsInFinalizeWindow)

                    <div class="steal-countdown-card steal-countdown-card--finalize">

                            </p>

                    </div>
                }

            @* Steal pending checkout notice — visible to everyone *@

                    <p class="detail-seller__name">@sellerDisplay</p>
                    <p class="detail-seller__since">
                        Member since @(Model.User?.CreatedAt.ToString("MMMM yyyy") ?? "—")
                    </p>

            @* ── Action buttons ──────────────────────────────────────────────── *@

            @* ── 1. Owner ──────────────────────────────────────────────── *@
            @if (isOwner)
            {
                <div class="detail-actions">

            else if (isAnonymous)
            {
                <div class="detail-actions">

                       asp-route-returnUrl="@Context.Request.Path"

                    <a asp-action="Login" asp-controller="Auth"

            else

                                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.704 4.153a.75.75 0 01.143 1.052l-8 10.5a.75.75 0 01-1.127.075l-4.5-4.5a.75.75 0 011.06-1.06l3.894 3.893 7.48-9.817a.75.75 0 011.05-.143z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                </svg>
                                Get this Item
                            </button>
                        </form>
                    </div>
                    <p class="detail-steal-explainer">
                        Claiming this item reserves it at the base price. Another buyer can Steal it
                        — adding ₱50 — within the @Model.StealDurationHours-hour window.
                        If no one steals it, the item is yours to finalise.
                    </p>
                }

                @* ══ 3c. Stealable — Reserved (original getter) ══ *@
                else if (Model.Status == ItemStatus.Reserved)
                {
                    @if (isCurrentWinner)
                    {
                        @if (Model.IsInFinalizeWindow)
                        {
                            <div class="detail-actions">
                                <a asp-action="Checkout" asp-controller="Orders" asp-route-itemId="@Model.Id"
                                   class="detail-btn detail-btn--complete">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" width="18" height="18">
                                        <path d="M2.003 5.884L10 9.882l7.997-3.998A2 2 0 0016 4H4a2 2 0 00-1.997 1.884z" />
                                        <path d="M18 8.118l-8 4-8-4V14a2 2 0 002 2h12a2 2 0 002-2V8.118z" />
                                    </svg>
                                    Complete Purchase
                                </a>
                            </div>
                            <p class="detail-steal-explainer detail-steal-explainer--winner">
                                The steal window has closed — the item is yours! Finalise your
                                purchase before your 2-hour grace period expires.
                            </p>
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            <div class="detail-actions detail-actions--waiting">
                                <div class="detail-winner-notice">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                                        <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm3.857-9.809a.75.75 0 00-1.214-.882l-3.483 4.79-1.88-1.88a.75.75 0 10-1.06 1.061l2.5 2.5a.75.75 0 001.137-.089l4-5.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                    </svg>
                                    <span>You hold this item at <strong>₱@Model.Price.ToString("N2")</strong>. Watch the countdown — if no one steals it, you can finalise once the timer hits zero.</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>

                            @* Cancel Get widget — only shown while steal window is still open *@
                            <div class="detail-cancel-get-wrap">
                                <p class="detail-cancel-get-hint">Changed your mind?</p>
                                <form asp-action="CancelGet" asp-controller="Items" asp-route-id="@Model.Id" method="post">
                                    @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                    <button type="submit" class="detail-cancel-get-btn">
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true">
                                            <path d="M6.28 5.22a.75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06L8.94 10l-3.72 3.72a.75.75 0 101.06 1.06L10 11.06l3.72 3.72a.75.75 0 101.06-1.06L11.06 10l3.72-3.72a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06L10 8.94 6.28 5.22z" />
                                        </svg>
                                        Cancel reservation
                                    </button>
                                </form>
                                <p class="detail-cancel-get-note">
                                    Cancelling releases your reservation and returns the item to available so anyone can claim it.
                                </p>
                            </div>
                        }
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        @if (stealWindowOpen)
                        {
                            <div class="detail-actions">
                                <form asp-action="StealItem" asp-controller="Items" asp-route-id="@Model.Id" method="post">
                                    @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                    <button type="submit" class="detail-btn detail-btn--steal">
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" width="18" height="18">
                                            <path d="M10 12a2 2 0 100-4 2 2 0 000 4z" />
                                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M.458 10C1.732 5.943 5.522 3 10 3s8.268 2.943 9.542 7c-1.274 4.057-5.064 7-9.542 7S1.732 14.057.458 10zM14 10a4 4 0 11-8 0 4 4 0 018 0z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                        </svg>
                                        Steal this Item
                                        <span class="detail-btn__badge">+₱50</span>
                                    </button>
                                </form>
                            </div>
                            <p class="detail-steal-explainer">
                                Someone has already claimed this item. Steal it now — the price
                                jumps by ₱50. You'll be sent to checkout to complete the purchase.
                                You can cancel the steal at checkout if you change your mind.
                            </p>
                        }
                        else if (Model.IsInFinalizeWindow)
                        {
                            <div class="detail-actions detail-actions--waiting">
                                <div class="detail-locked-notice">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                                        <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 1a4.5 4.5 0 00-4.5 4.5V9H5a2 2 0 00-2 2v6a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-6a2 2 0 00-2-2h-.5V5.5A4.5 4.5 0 0010 1zm3 8V5.5a3 3 0 10-6 0V9h6z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                    </svg>
                                    <span>The steal window has closed. The original buyer is finalising their purchase.</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            <div class="detail-actions">
                                <button type="button" class="detail-btn detail-btn--buy" disabled>Unavailable</button>
                            </div>
                        }
                    }
                }

                @* ══ 3d. Stealable — StolenPendingCheckout ══
                         The stealer has bumped the price and is mid-checkout.
                         They can complete or cancel. Others see a waiting notice. *@
                else if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.StolenPendingCheckout)
                {
                    @if (isCurrentWinner)
                    {
                        <div class="detail-actions">
                            <a asp-action="Checkout" asp-controller="Orders" asp-route-itemId="@Model.Id"
                               class="detail-btn detail-btn--complete">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" width="18" height="18">
                                    <path d="M2.003 5.884L10 9.882l7.997-3.998A2 2 0 0016 4H4a2 2 0 00-1.997 1.884z" />
                                    <path d="M18 8.118l-8 4-8-4V14a2 2 0 002 2h12a2 2 0 002-2V8.118z" />
                                </svg>
                                Complete Purchase
                            </a>
                        </div>
                        <p class="detail-steal-explainer detail-steal-explainer--winner">
                            You stole this item at ₱@Model.Price.ToString("N2"). Complete your
                            purchase to secure it — or cancel at checkout to return it to available.
                        </p>
                    }
                    else if (isOriginalGetter)
                    {
                        @* Original getter: reassure them their reservation is intact *@
                        <div class="detail-actions detail-actions--waiting">
                            <div class="detail-winner-notice">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm.75-13a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v5c0 .414.336.75.75.75h4a.75.75 0 000-1.5h-3.25V5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                </svg>
                                <span>Someone is stealing your item at the higher price. If they don't complete checkout, your reservation will be fully restored automatically.</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        <div class="detail-actions detail-actions--waiting">
                            <div class="detail-locked-notice">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 1a4.5 4.5 0 00-4.5 4.5V9H5a2 2 0 00-2 2v6a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-6a2 2 0 00-2-2h-.5V5.5A4.5 4.5 0 0010 1zm3 8V5.5a3 3 0 10-6 0V9h6z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                </svg>
                                <span>A buyer is completing a steal purchase. If they cancel, the item returns to its previous holder.</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    }
                }

                @if (TempData["InfoMessage"] is string infoMsg)
                {
                    <div class="create-toast create-toast--info">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M18 10a8 8 0 11-16 0 8 8 0 0116 0zm-7-4a1 1 0 11-2 0 1 1 0 012 0zM9 9a.75.75 0 000 1.5h.253a.25.25 0 01.244.304l-.459 2.066A1.75 1.75 0 0010.747 15H11a.75.75 0 000-1.5h-.253a.25.25 0 01-.244-.304l.459-2.066A1.75 1.75 0 009.253 9H9z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        @infoMsg
                    </div>
                }

                @* ══ 3e. Stealable — Sold (order confirmed) ══ *@
                else if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.Sold)
                {
                    @* Sold notice is rendered above; no button needed unless still pending *@
                }


            }

        </section>

    </div>

</div>
