            <div class="ic-field ic-field--full">
                <label class="ic-field__label" for="itemDesc">Description</label>
                <textarea id="itemDesc" class="ic-field__textarea" rows="4"
                          placeholder="Describe the item — material, fit, notable features..." maxlength="1000"></textarea>
                <p class="ic-field__error" id="errDesc" hidden></p>
            </div>

            <div class="ic-field">
                <label class="ic-field__label" for="itemCategory">Category</label>
                <select id="itemCategory" class="ic-field__select">
                    <option value="">Select category…</option>
                    @foreach (var cat in ItemConstants.Categories)
                    {
                        <option value="@cat">@cat</option>
                    }
                </select>
                <p class="ic-field__error" id="errCategory" hidden></p>
            </div>

            <div class="ic-field">
                <label class="ic-field__label" for="itemCondition">Condition</label>
                <select id="itemCondition" class="ic-field__select">
                    <option value="">Select condition…</option>
                    @foreach (var cond in ItemConstants.Conditions)
                    {
                        <option value="@cond">@cond</option>
                    }
                </select>
                <p class="ic-field__error" id="errCondition" hidden></p>
            </div>

        </div>
    </div>

    @* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ *@
    @* SECTION 2 — Images                                                    *@
    @* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ *@
    <div class="ic-card">
        <div class="ic-card__label">Images <span class="ic-card__label-hint">Up to @ItemConstants.MaxImagesPerListing · First image is the cover</span></div>

        <div class="ic-images" id="imageGrid">
            @* Image slots rendered by JS *@
        </div>
        <p class="ic-field__error" id="errImages" hidden></p>
    </div>

    @* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ *@
    @* SECTION 3 — Variants                                                  *@
    @* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ *@
    <div class="ic-card">
        <div class="ic-card__label-row">
            <div>
                <div class="ic-card__label">Variants</div>
                <p class="ic-card__label-hint ic-card__label-hint--block">
                    Each variant is a colour, style, or option. Add sizes and quantities under each.
                </p>
            </div>
            <button type="button" class="tl-btn tl-btn--ghost ic-add-variant" id="addVariantBtn">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="13" height="13" aria-hidden="true">
                    <path d="M7.75 2a.75.75 0 01.75.75V7h4.25a.75.75 0 010 1.5H8.5v4.25a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0V8.5H2.75a.75.75 0 010-1.5H7V2.75A.75.75 0 017.75 2z" />
                </svg>
                Add Variant
            </button>
        </div>

        <div id="variantList" class="ic-variant-list"></div>
        <p class="ic-field__error" id="errVariants" hidden></p>
    </div>

    @* ── Publish ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── *@
    <div class="ic-footer">
        <a asp-controller="Shop" asp-action="Mine" class="tl-btn tl-btn--ghost">Cancel</a>
        <button type="button" class="tl-btn tl-btn--primary" id="publishBtn">
            Publish Item
        </button>
    </div>

</div>

@* ── SKU row template (cloned by JS, kept hidden) ─────────────────────────── *@
<template id="skuTemplate">
    <div class="ic-sku-row">
        <select class="ic-field__select ic-sku__size">
            <option value="">No size</option>
            @foreach (var sz in ItemConstants.Sizes)
            {
                <option value="@sz">@sz</option>
            }
        </select>
        <div class="ic-sku__price-wrap">
            <span class="ic-sku__currency">₱</span>
            <input type="number" class="ic-field__input ic-sku__price"
                   placeholder="0.00" min="0.01" step="0.01" />
        </div>
        <input type="number" class="ic-field__input ic-sku__qty"
               placeholder="Qty" min="1" max="9999" step="1" />
        <button type="button" class="ic-sku__remove" aria-label="Remove SKU">
            <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="13" height="13">
                <path d="M3.72 3.72a.75.75 0 011.06 0L8 6.94l3.22-3.22a.75.75 0 111.06 1.06L9.06 8l3.22 3.22a.75.75 0 11-1.06 1.06L8 9.06l-3.22 3.22a.75.75 0 01-1.06-1.06L6.94 8 3.72 4.78a.75.75 0 010-1.06z" />
            </svg>
        </button>
    </div>
</template>

<script>
    (function () {
        'use strict';

        const AF_TOKEN      = document.getElementById('afToken').value;
        const SHOP_ID       = parseInt(document.getElementById('shopId').value);
        const MAX_IMAGES    = @ItemConstants.MaxImagesPerListing;
        const MAX_VARIANTS  = 10;

        const CREATE_URL     = '/Shop/Create';
        const IMG_UPLOAD_URL = '/Shop/SaveListingImage';

        // ── State ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        const imageFiles  = new Array(MAX_IMAGES).fill(null); // File | null per slot
        let   variantCount = 0;

        // ── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        function showError(elId, msg) {
            const el = document.getElementById(elId);
            if (!el) return;
            el.textContent = msg;
            el.hidden = !msg;
        }

        function showGlobal(msg) {
            const banner = document.getElementById('globalError');
            document.getElementById('globalErrorText').textContent = msg;
            banner.hidden = !msg;
            if (msg) banner.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest' });
        }

        async function postJson(url, body) {
            const res = await fetch(url, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    'RequestVerificationToken': AF_TOKEN
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(body)
            });
            return res.json();
        }

        async function uploadFile(url, formData) {
            const res = await fetch(url, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'RequestVerificationToken': AF_TOKEN },
                body: formData
            });
            return res.json();
        }

        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  IMAGE SLOTS
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        const imageGrid = document.getElementById('imageGrid');

        function renderImageSlots() {
            imageGrid.innerHTML = '';
            for (let i = 0; i < MAX_IMAGES; i++) {
                const slot = document.createElement('label');
                slot.className = 'ic-image-slot' + (i === 0 ? ' ic-image-slot--cover' : '');
                slot.title = i === 0 ? 'Cover image' : `Image ${i + 1}`;

                const input = document.createElement('input');
                input.type   = 'file';
                input.accept = 'image/jpeg,image/png,image/webp,image/gif';
                input.className = 'ic-image-slot__input';
                input.dataset.slot = i;

                if (imageFiles[i]) {
                    const img = document.createElement('img');
                    img.src   = URL.createObjectURL(imageFiles[i]);
                    img.className = 'ic-image-slot__preview';
                    slot.appendChild(img);
                    if (i === 0) {
                        const badge = document.createElement('span');
                        badge.className = 'ic-image-slot__badge';
                        badge.textContent = 'Cover';
                        slot.appendChild(badge);
                    }
                } else {
                    const icon = document.createElement('div');
                    icon.className = 'ic-image-slot__empty';
                    icon.innerHTML = `
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5"
                             width="22" height="22" aria-hidden="true">
                            <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"
                                  d="M12 16.5V9.75m0 0l3 3m-3-3l-3 3M6.75 19.5a4.5 4.5 0
                                     01-1.41-8.775 5.25 5.25 0 0110.233-2.33 3 3 0
                                     013.758 3.848A3.752 3.752 0 0118 19.5H6.75z"/>
                        </svg>
                        <span>${i === 0 ? 'Cover' : '+'}</span>`;
                    slot.appendChild(icon);
                }

                input.addEventListener('change', () => {
                    const file = input.files[0];
                    if (!file) return;
                    if (file.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) {
                        showError('errImages', `Image ${i + 1} exceeds 5 MB.`);
                        return;
                    }
                    showError('errImages', '');
                    imageFiles[i] = file;
                    renderImageSlots();
                });

                slot.appendChild(input);
                imageGrid.appendChild(slot);
            }
        }

        renderImageSlots();

        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  VARIANT BUILDER
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        const variantList   = document.getElementById('variantList');
        const addVariantBtn = document.getElementById('addVariantBtn');
        const skuTemplate   = document.getElementById('skuTemplate');

        function addVariant() {
            if (variantCount >= MAX_VARIANTS) {
                showError('errVariants', `Maximum ${MAX_VARIANTS} variants allowed.`);
                return;
            }

            const vid   = ++variantCount;
            const card  = document.createElement('div');
            card.className   = 'ic-variant-card';
            card.dataset.vid = vid;

            card.innerHTML = `
                <div class="ic-variant-header">
                    <div class="ic-field" style="flex:1">
                        <label class="ic-field__label" for="vname-${vid}">Variant Name</label>
                        <input id="vname-${vid}" type="text" class="ic-field__input ic-variant__name"
                               placeholder="e.g. Red, Navy, Classic Fit" maxlength="50" />
                        <p class="ic-field__error ic-variant__name-error" hidden></p>
                    </div>
                    <button type="button" class="ic-variant__remove" aria-label="Remove variant">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14">
                            <path d="M11 1.75V3h2.25a.75.75 0 010 1.5H2.75a.75.75 0 010-1.5H5V1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h2.5C10.216 0 11 .784 11 1.75zM4.496 6.675a.75.75 0 10-1.492.15l.66 6.6A1.75 1.75 0 005.405 15h5.19a1.75 1.75 0 001.741-1.575l.66-6.6a.75.75 0 10-1.492-.15l-.66 6.6a.25.25 0 01-.249.225H5.405a.25.25 0 01-.249-.225l-.66-6.6z"/>
                        </svg>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <div class="ic-sku-list">
                    <div class="ic-sku-header">
                        <span>Size</span><span>Price</span><span>Quantity</span><span></span>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <button type="button" class="tl-btn tl-btn--ghost ic-add-sku">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="12" height="12">
                        <path d="M7.75 2a.75.75 0 01.75.75V7h4.25a.75.75 0 010 1.5H8.5v4.25a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0V8.5H2.75a.75.75 0 010-1.5H7V2.75A.75.75 0 017.75 2z"/>
                    </svg>
                    Add Size / SKU
                </button>
                <p class="ic-field__error ic-variant__sku-error" hidden></p>`;

            // Remove variant
            card.querySelector('.ic-variant__remove').addEventListener('click', () => {
                card.remove();
                showError('errVariants', '');
            });

            // Add SKU
            card.querySelector('.ic-add-sku').addEventListener('click', () => {
                addSku(card.querySelector('.ic-sku-list'));
            });

            variantList.appendChild(card);
            showError('errVariants', '');

            // Auto-add first SKU
            addSku(card.querySelector('.ic-sku-list'));

            card.querySelector('.ic-variant__name').focus();
        }

        function addSku(skuList) {
            const row = skuTemplate.content.cloneNode(true).querySelector('.ic-sku-row');
            row.querySelector('.ic-sku__remove').addEventListener('click', () => row.remove());
            skuList.appendChild(row);
        }

        addVariantBtn.addEventListener('click', addVariant);

        // Add one variant by default so the page isn't empty
        addVariant();

        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  VALIDATION
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        function validateAndBuild() {
            let valid = true;

            const title     = document.getElementById('itemTitle').value.trim();
            const desc      = document.getElementById('itemDesc').value.trim();
            const category  = document.getElementById('itemCategory').value;
            const condition = document.getElementById('itemCondition').value;

            showError('errTitle',    '');
            showError('errDesc',     '');
            showError('errCategory', '');
            showError('errCondition','');
            showError('errVariants', '');
            showError('errImages',   '');
            showGlobal('');

            if (!title)     { showError('errTitle',    'Title is required.');     valid = false; }
            if (!desc)      { showError('errDesc',     'Description is required.'); valid = false; }
            if (!category)  { showError('errCategory', 'Please select a category.'); valid = false; }
            if (!condition) { showError('errCondition','Please select a condition.'); valid = false; }

            if (imageFiles.filter(Boolean).length === 0) {
                showError('errImages', 'Add at least one image.');
                valid = false;
            }

            const variantCards = variantList.querySelectorAll('.ic-variant-card');
            if (variantCards.length === 0) {
                showError('errVariants', 'Add at least one variant.');
                valid = false;
            }

            const variants = [];
            variantCards.forEach(card => {
                const name    = card.querySelector('.ic-variant__name').value.trim();
                const nameErr = card.querySelector('.ic-variant__name-error');
                const skuErr  = card.querySelector('.ic-variant__sku-error');
                nameErr.hidden = true;
                skuErr.hidden  = true;

                if (!name) {
                    nameErr.textContent = 'Variant name is required.';
                    nameErr.hidden = false;
                    valid = false;
                }

                const skus = [];
                card.querySelectorAll('.ic-sku-row').forEach(row => {
                    const size  = row.querySelector('.ic-sku__size').value;
                    const price = parseFloat(row.querySelector('.ic-sku__price').value);
                    const qty   = parseInt(row.querySelector('.ic-sku__qty').value, 10);

                    if (isNaN(price) || price <= 0) {
                        skuErr.textContent = 'All SKUs need a valid price.';
                        skuErr.hidden = false;
                        valid = false;
                        return;
                    }
                    if (isNaN(qty) || qty < 1) {
                        skuErr.textContent = 'All SKUs need a valid quantity.';
                        skuErr.hidden = false;
                        valid = false;
                        return;
                    }
                    skus.push({ size: size || null, price, quantity: qty });
                });

                if (skus.length === 0) {
                    skuErr.textContent = 'Add at least one SKU to this variant.';
                    skuErr.hidden = false;
                    valid = false;
                }

                variants.push({ name, skus });
            });

            if (!valid) return null;

            return { shopId: SHOP_ID, title, description: desc, category, condition, variants };
        }

        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  PUBLISH
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        document.getElementById('publishBtn').addEventListener('click', async () => {
            const payload = validateAndBuild();
            if (!payload) return;

            const btn = document.getElementById('publishBtn');
            btn.disabled    = true;
            btn.textContent = 'Publishing…';

            // Step 1 — create the item
            const createRes = await postJson(CREATE_URL, payload);
            if (!createRes.ok) {
                showGlobal(createRes.error ?? 'Failed to create item.');
                btn.disabled    = false;
                btn.textContent = 'Publish Item';
                return;
            }

            const itemId = createRes.itemId;

            // Step 2 — upload images sequentially
            const selectedFiles = imageFiles
                .map((f, i) => ({ file: f, slot: i }))
                .filter(x => x.file !== null);

            for (const { file, slot } of selectedFiles) {
                btn.textContent = `Uploading image ${slot + 1}…`;
                const fd = new FormData();
                fd.append('itemId', itemId);
                fd.append('slot',   slot);
                fd.append('file',   file);
                const imgRes = await uploadFile(IMG_UPLOAD_URL, fd);
                if (!imgRes.ok) {
                    // Image failed but item was created — still redirect, warn user
                    showGlobal(`Item created but image ${slot + 1} failed: ${imgRes.error}`);
                    btn.disabled    = false;
                    btn.textContent = 'Publish Item';
                    return;
                }
            }

            // Step 3 — redirect to shop page
            window.location.href = `/Shop/Mine`;
        });

    }());
</script>

        max-width: 760px;

        padding: 1.5rem 1.25rem 4rem;

    }

    /* ── Grid ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

    }

    /* ── Fields ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
    .ic-field {

        gap: 0.375rem;
    }

    .ic-field__label {
        font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
        font-size: 0.875rem;
        font-weight: 600;
        color: var(--color-text, #1a1814);
    }

    .ic-field__input,
    .ic-field__textarea,
    .ic-field__select {
        padding: 0.75rem 0.875rem;
        border: 1.5px solid var(--color-border, #e2ddd6);
        border-radius: 8px;
        font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
        font-size: 0.9rem;
        color: var(--color-text, #1a1814);
        background: #fff;
        outline: none;
        transition: border-color 0.15s;
        width: 100%;
        box-sizing: border-box;
    }

    .ic-field__textarea {
        resize: vertical;
        min-height: 100px;
    }

        .ic-field__input:focus,
        .ic-field__textarea:focus,
        .ic-field__select:focus {
            border-color: var(--color-primary, #2d5a27);
        }

    .ic-field__error {
        font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
        font-size: 0.8rem;
        color: #dc2626;
        margin: 0;
    }

    /* ── Image slots ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
    .ic-images {
        display: grid;
        grid-template-columns: repeat(5, 1fr);
        gap: 0.75rem;
    }

    .ic-image-slot {
        aspect-ratio: 1;
        border: 2px dashed var(--color-border, #e2ddd6);
        border-radius: 10px;
        cursor: pointer;
        overflow: hidden;
        position: relative;
        display: flex;
        align-items: center;
        justify-content: center;
        transition: border-color 0.15s, background 0.15s;
    }

        .ic-image-slot:hover {
            border-color: var(--color-primary, #2d5a27);
            background: color-mix(in srgb, var(--color-primary, #2d5a27) 4%, transparent);
        }

    .ic-image-slot--cover {
        border-style: solid;
        border-color: var(--color-primary, #2d5a27);
    }

    .ic-image-slot__input {
        position: absolute;
        width: 1px;
        height: 1px;
        opacity: 0;
        pointer-events: none;
    }

    .ic-image-slot__preview {
        width: 100%;
        height: 100%;
        object-fit: cover;
    }

    .ic-image-slot__badge {
        position: absolute;
        bottom: 4px;
        left: 4px;
        background: var(--color-primary, #2d5a27);
        color: #fff;
        font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
        font-size: 0.65rem;
        font-weight: 700;
        padding: 2px 6px;
        border-radius: 4px;
    }

    .ic-image-slot__empty {
        display: flex;
        flex-direction: column;
        align-items: center;
        gap: 4px;
        color: var(--color-muted, #8a8278);
        pointer-events: none;
    }

        .ic-image-slot__empty span {
            font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
            font-size: 0.75rem;
            font-weight: 600;
        }

    /* ── Variant list ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
    .ic-variant-list {
        display: flex;
        flex-direction: column;
        gap: 1rem;
    }

    .ic-variant-card {
        border: 1px solid var(--color-border, #e2ddd6);
        border-radius: 10px;
        padding: 1rem;
        display: flex;

        gap: 0.875rem;
    }

    .ic-variant-header {
        display: flex;
        align-items: flex-end;
        gap: 0.75rem;
    }

    .ic-variant__remove {
        flex-shrink: 0;
        background: none;
        border: none;
        cursor: pointer;
        color: var(--color-muted, #8a8278);

        border-radius: 6px;
        display: flex;
        align-items: center;
        margin-bottom: 2px;
    }

        .ic-variant__remove:hover {
            color: #dc2626;
            background: #fee2e2;
        }

    /* SKU table */
    .ic-sku-header {
        display: grid;
        grid-template-columns: 2fr 2fr 1.5fr 36px;
        gap: 0.5rem;
        font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
        font-size: 0.75rem;
        font-weight: 700;
        color: var(--color-muted, #8a8278);
        text-transform: uppercase;
        letter-spacing: 0.05em;
        padding: 0 0 0.375rem;
    }

    .ic-sku-row {
        display: grid;
        grid-template-columns: 2fr 2fr 1.5fr 36px;
        gap: 0.5rem;
        align-items: center;
        margin-bottom: 0.5rem;
    }

    .ic-sku__price-wrap {
        display: flex;
        align-items: center;
        border: 1.5px solid var(--color-border, #e2ddd6);
        border-radius: 8px;
        overflow: hidden;
        transition: border-color 0.15s;
    }

        .ic-sku__price-wrap:focus-within {
            border-color: var(--color-primary, #2d5a27);
        }

    .ic-sku__currency {
        padding: 0 0.625rem;
        font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
        font-size: 0.9rem;
        color: var(--color-muted, #8a8278);

@model ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ShopItemDetailsViewModel

<div class="detail-shell">

                         class="detail-shop-pill__logo" />

                        @char.ToUpper(Model.ShopName.FirstOrDefault())
                    </div>

                    <span class="detail-shop-pill__label">Sold by</span>

                     class="detail-shop-pill__chevron" aria-hidden="true">
                    <path d="M6.22 3.22a.75.75 0 011.06 0l4.25 4.25a.75.75 0 010 1.06l-4.25 4.25a.75.75 0 01-1.06-1.06L9.94 8 6.22 4.28a.75.75 0 010-1.06z" />
                </svg>
            </a>

        </aside>

        @* ════════════════════════ RIGHT — Details ════════════════════════════ *@
        <section class="detail-info-col">

            <div class="detail-meta-row">
                <span class="detail-category">@Model.Category</span>
                <span class="detail-condition @condClass">@Model.Condition</span>
                <span class="detail-listing-type-badge">Shop</span>
            </div>

            <h1 class="detail-title">@Model.Title</h1>

            <div class="detail-price-block">
                <span class="detail-price" id="selectedPrice">
                    ₱@Model.StartingPrice.ToString("N2")

            @if (Model.Variants.Count > 0)
            {
                <div class="vp-shell">

                    @* Step 1: pick a variant *@
                    <div class="vp-section">
                        <p class="vp-section__label">
                            Variant
                            <span class="vp-section__required" id="variantRequired" hidden>
                                — please select one
                            </span>
                        </p>
                        <div class="vp-variant-chips" id="variantChips">
                            @foreach (var v in Model.Variants)
                            {
                                <button type="button"
                                        class="vp-chip"
                                        data-variant-id="@v.VariantId">
                                    @v.Name
                                </button>

                                — please select one

                    </div>

                </div>

                @* Variant data embedded as JSON for the JS picker *@
                <script id="variantData" type="application/json">
                    @Html.Raw(System.Text.Json.JsonSerializer.Serialize(
                        Model.Variants.Select(v => new {
                            variantId = v.VariantId,
                            name      = v.Name,
                            skus      = v.Skus.Select(s => new {
                                skuId       = s.SkuId,
                                size        = s.Size,
                                price       = s.Price,
                                quantity    = s.Quantity,
                                isAvailable = s.IsAvailable
                            })
                        })
                    ))
                </script>

            @* ── Action buttons ───────────────────────────────────────────── *@
            <div class="detail-actions" id="detailActions">
                @if (Model.IsOwner)
                {
                    <a asp-controller="Shop" asp-action="Edit"

                       class="tl-btn tl-btn--ghost detail-actions__btn">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="13" height="13">

                        </svg>

                            id="addToCartBtn" style="width:100%">

            @if (TempData["SuccessMessage"] is string okMsg)
            {
                <p class="detail-flash detail-flash--success">@okMsg</p>
            }

        </section>
    </div>
</div>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
    (function () {
        const rawData = document.getElementById('variantData');
        if (!rawData) return;

        const variants      = JSON.parse(rawData.textContent);
        const variantChips  = document.getElementById('variantChips');
        const skuSection    = document.getElementById('skuSection');
        const skuChips      = document.getElementById('skuChips');
        const priceEl       = document.getElementById('selectedPrice');
        const priceLabelEl  = document.getElementById('priceLabel');
        const variantReqEl  = document.getElementById('variantRequired');
        const skuReqEl      = document.getElementById('skuRequired');

        let selectedVariantId = null;
        let selectedSkuId     = null;

        // ── Variant chip click ────────────────────────────────────────────
        variantChips?.addEventListener('click', e => {
            const chip = e.target.closest('.vp-chip');
            if (!chip) return;

            variantChips.querySelectorAll('.vp-chip').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('vp-chip--active'));
            chip.classList.add('vp-chip--active');

            selectedVariantId = parseInt(chip.dataset.variantId);
            selectedSkuId     = null;
            variantReqEl.hidden = true;

            const variant = variants.find(v => v.variantId === selectedVariantId);
            if (!variant) return;

            // Render SKU chips
            skuChips.innerHTML = '';
            variant.skus.forEach(sku => {
                const btn = document.createElement('button');
                btn.type             = 'button';
                btn.className        = 'vp-chip' + (sku.isAvailable ? '' : ' vp-chip--disabled');
                btn.dataset.skuId    = sku.skuId;
                btn.dataset.price    = sku.price;
                btn.dataset.qty      = sku.quantity;
                btn.disabled         = !sku.isAvailable;
                btn.textContent      = sku.size || 'One size';
                if (!sku.isAvailable) btn.title = 'Out of stock';
                skuChips.appendChild(btn);
            });

            skuSection.removeAttribute('hidden');

            // Reset price display
            const lowestAvailable = variant.skus
                .filter(s => s.isAvailable)
                .reduce((min, s) => s.price < min ? s.price : min, Infinity);

            if (lowestAvailable < Infinity) {
                priceEl.textContent = '₱' + lowestAvailable.toLocaleString('en-PH', { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
                priceLabelEl.textContent = 'Starting price';
            }
        });

        // ── SKU chip click ────────────────────────────────────────────────
        skuChips?.addEventListener('click', e => {
            const chip = e.target.closest('.vp-chip:not(.vp-chip--disabled)');
            if (!chip) return;

            skuChips.querySelectorAll('.vp-chip').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('vp-chip--active'));
            chip.classList.add('vp-chip--active');

            selectedSkuId = parseInt(chip.dataset.skuId);
            skuReqEl.hidden = true;

            priceEl.textContent = '₱' + parseFloat(chip.dataset.price)
                .toLocaleString('en-PH', { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
            priceLabelEl.textContent = `${chip.dataset.qty} available`;
        });

        // ── Gallery ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        const mainImg  = document.getElementById('mainGalleryImg');
        const thumbs   = document.querySelectorAll('.gallery-thumb');
        const counter  = document.getElementById('galleryCounter');
        const prevBtn  = document.getElementById('galleryPrev');
        const nextBtn  = document.getElementById('galleryNext');

        const urls = Array.from(thumbs).map(t => t.dataset.src);
        let current = 0;

        function goTo(idx) {
            if (!mainImg || urls.length === 0) return;
            current = (idx + urls.length) % urls.length;
            mainImg.src = urls[current];
            thumbs.forEach((t, i) => t.classList.toggle('gallery-thumb--active', i === current));
            if (counter) counter.textContent = `${current + 1} / ${urls.length}`;
        }

        thumbs.forEach((t, i) => t.addEventListener('click', () => goTo(i)));
        prevBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => goTo(current - 1));
        nextBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => goTo(current + 1));

    }());
    </script>
}

        font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
        font-size: 0.7rem;
        font-weight: 700;
        letter-spacing: .05em;
        text-transform: uppercase;
        padding: 2px 8px;
        border-radius: 999px;
        background: color-mix(in srgb, var(--color-primary, #2d5a27) 12%, transparent);
        color: var(--color-primary, #2d5a27);
    }
</style>


--- Views/Shop/Details.cshtml.cs ---

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;

namespace ThriftLoop.Views.Shop
{
    public class DetailsModel : PageModel
    {
        public void OnGet()
        {
        }
    }
}



--- Views/Shop/Edit.cshtml ---

@model ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ShopItemEditViewModel
@using ThriftLoop.ViewModels
@using ThriftLoop.Constants
@inject Microsoft.AspNetCore.Antiforgery.IAntiforgery Antiforgery

@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Edit — " + Model.Title;
    Layout = "~/Views/Shared/_Layout.cshtml";
    var afToken = Antiforgery.GetAndStoreTokens(Context).RequestToken ?? string.Empty;

    // Serialize existing variant data for JS pre-population
    var variantJson = System.Text.Json.JsonSerializer.Serialize(
        Model.Variants.Select(v => new
        {
            variantId = v.VariantId,
            name = v.Name,
            skus = v.Skus.Select(s => new
            {
                skuId = s.SkuId,
                size = s.Size,
                price = s.Price,
                quantity = s.Quantity
            })
        })
    );
}

<div class="ic-shell">

    <nav class="detail-breadcrumb" aria-label="Breadcrumb">
        <a asp-controller="Shop" asp-action="Details" asp-route-id="@Model.ItemId"
           class="detail-breadcrumb__link">
            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" aria-hidden="true">
                <path d="M12.5 5L7.5 10L12.5 15" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
            </svg>
            Back to listing
        </a>
    </nav>

    <div class="ic-header">
        <h1 class="ic-header__title">Edit Listing</h1>
        <p class="ic-header__sub">@Model.ShopName</p>
    </div>

    <div class="ic-alert ic-alert--error" id="globalError" hidden>
        <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="15" height="15" aria-hidden="true">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8 15A7 7 0 108 1a7 7 0 000 14zm-.75-9.25a.75.75 0 011.5 0v4a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0v-4zm.75 7.5a1 1 0 100-2 1 1 0 000 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
        </svg>
        <span id="globalErrorText"></span>
    </div>

    <input type="hidden" id="afToken" value="@afToken" />
    <input type="hidden" id="itemId" value="@Model.ItemId" />
    <input type="hidden" id="shopId" value="@Model.ShopId" />

    @* ══ Item Details ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ *@
    <div class="ic-card">
        <div class="ic-card__label">Item Details</div>
        <div class="ic-grid">

            <div class="ic-field ic-field--full">
                <label class="ic-field__label" for="itemTitle">Title</label>
                <input id="itemTitle" type="text" class="ic-field__input"
                       value="@Model.Title" maxlength="100" />
                <p class="ic-field__error" id="errTitle" hidden></p>
            </div>

            <div class="ic-field ic-field--full">
                <label class="ic-field__label" for="itemDesc">Description</label>
                <textarea id="itemDesc" class="ic-field__textarea" rows="4"
                          maxlength="1000">@Model.Description</textarea>
                <p class="ic-field__error" id="errDesc" hidden></p>
            </div>

            <div class="ic-field">
                <label class="ic-field__label" for="itemCategory">Category</label>
                <select id="itemCategory" class="ic-field__select">
                    @foreach (var cat in ShopItemEditViewModel.Categories)
                    {
                        @if (Model.Category == cat)
                        {
                            <option value="@cat" selected>@cat</option>
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            <option value="@cat">@cat</option>
                        }
                    }
                </select>
                <p class="ic-field__error" id="errCategory" hidden></p>
            </div>

            <div class="ic-field">
                <label class="ic-field__label" for="itemCondition">Condition</label>
                <select id="itemCondition" class="ic-field__select">
                    @foreach (var cond in ShopItemEditViewModel.Conditions)
                    {
                        @if (Model.Condition == cond)
                        {
                            <option value="@cond" selected>@cond</option>
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            <option value="@cond">@cond</option>
                        }
                    }
                </select>
                <p class="ic-field__error" id="errCondition" hidden></p>
            </div>

        </div>
    </div>

    @* ══ Images ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ *@
    <div class="ic-card">
        <div class="ic-card__label">
            Images
            <span class="ic-card__label-hint">Up to @ItemConstants.MaxImagesPerListing · Changes save immediately</span>
        </div>
        <div class="ic-images" id="imageGrid"></div>
        <p class="ic-field__error" id="errImages" hidden></p>
    </div>

    @* ══ Variants ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ *@
    <div class="ic-card">
        <div class="ic-card__label-row">
            <div>
                <div class="ic-card__label">Variants</div>
                <p class="ic-card__label-hint ic-card__label-hint--block">
                    Removed variants with existing orders will have their stock zeroed instead of deleted.
                </p>
            </div>
            <button type="button" class="tl-btn tl-btn--ghost" id="addVariantBtn">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="13" height="13" aria-hidden="true">
                    <path d="M7.75 2a.75.75 0 01.75.75V7h4.25a.75.75 0 010 1.5H8.5v4.25a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0V8.5H2.75a.75.75 0 010-1.5H7V2.75A.75.75 0 017.75 2z" />
                </svg>
                Add Variant
            </button>
        </div>
        <div id="variantList" class="ic-variant-list"></div>
        <p class="ic-field__error" id="errVariants" hidden></p>
    </div>

    <div class="ic-footer">
        <a asp-controller="Shop" asp-action="Details" asp-route-id="@Model.ItemId"
           class="tl-btn tl-btn--ghost">Cancel</a>
        <button type="button" class="tl-btn tl-btn--primary" id="saveBtn">Save Changes</button>
    </div>

</div>

@* SKU row template *@
<template id="skuTemplate">
    <div class="ic-sku-row">
        <select class="ic-field__select ic-sku__size">
            <option value="">No size</option>
            @foreach (var sz in ShopItemEditViewModel.Sizes)
            {
                <option value="@sz">@sz</option>
            }
        </select>
        <div class="ic-sku__price-wrap">
            <span class="ic-sku__currency">₱</span>
            <input type="number" class="ic-field__input ic-sku__price"
                   placeholder="0.00" min="0.01" step="0.01" />
        </div>
        <input type="number" class="ic-field__input ic-sku__qty"
               placeholder="Qty" min="1" max="9999" step="1" />
        <button type="button" class="ic-sku__remove" aria-label="Remove SKU">
            <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="13" height="13">
                <path d="M3.72 3.72a.75.75 0 011.06 0L8 6.94l3.22-3.22a.75.75 0 111.06 1.06L9.06 8l3.22 3.22a.75.75 0 11-1.06 1.06L8 9.06l-3.22 3.22a.75.75 0 01-1.06-1.06L6.94 8 3.72 4.78a.75.75 0 010-1.06z" />
            </svg>
        </button>
    </div>
</template>

<script>
    (function () {
        'use strict';

        const AF_TOKEN         = document.getElementById('afToken').value;
        const ITEM_ID          = parseInt(document.getElementById('itemId').value);
        const MAX_IMAGES       = @ItemConstants.MaxImagesPerListing;
        const EDIT_URL         = '/Shop/Edit';
        const IMG_UPLOAD_URL   = '/Shop/SaveListingImage';
        const IMG_REMOVE_URL   = '/Shop/RemoveListingImage';

        // ── Existing data from server ─────────────────────────────────────────
        const EXISTING_VARIANTS = @Html.Raw(variantJson);
        const EXISTING_IMAGES   = @Html.Raw(System.Text.Json.JsonSerializer.Serialize(Model.ImageUrls));

        // ── Image state ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        // Each slot: { type: 'existing'|'new'|'empty', url?: string, file?: File }
        const imageSlots = [];

        for (let i = 0; i < MAX_IMAGES; i++) {
            if (i < EXISTING_IMAGES.length && EXISTING_IMAGES[i]) {
                imageSlots.push({ type: 'existing', url: EXISTING_IMAGES[i] });
            } else {
                imageSlots.push({ type: 'empty' });
            }
        }

        // ── Helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        function showError(id, msg) {
            const el = document.getElementById(id);
            if (!el) return;
            el.textContent = msg;
            el.hidden = !msg;
        }

        function showGlobal(msg) {
            const banner = document.getElementById('globalError');
            document.getElementById('globalErrorText').textContent = msg;
            banner.hidden = !msg;
            if (msg) banner.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest' });
        }

        async function postJson(url, body) {
            const res = await fetch(url, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'RequestVerificationToken': AF_TOKEN },
                body: JSON.stringify(body)
            });
            return res.json();
        }

        async function postForm(url, fd) {
            const res = await fetch(url, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'RequestVerificationToken': AF_TOKEN },
                body: fd
            });
            return res.json();
        }

        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  IMAGE GRID
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        const imageGrid = document.getElementById('imageGrid');

        function renderImageGrid() {
            imageGrid.innerHTML = '';
            imageSlots.forEach((slot, i) => {
                const label = document.createElement('label');
                label.className = 'ic-image-slot' + (i === 0 ? ' ic-image-slot--cover' : '');

                if (slot.type === 'empty') {
                    // File picker
                    const input = document.createElement('input');
                    input.type = 'file';
                    input.accept = 'image/jpeg,image/png,image/webp,image/gif';
                    input.className = 'ic-image-slot__input';
                    input.addEventListener('change', () => handleNewImage(i, input.files[0]));
                    label.appendChild(input);

                    const empty = document.createElement('div');
                    empty.className = 'ic-image-slot__empty';
                    empty.innerHTML = `<svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor"
                        stroke-width="1.5" width="22" height="22">
                        <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"
                              d="M12 16.5V9.75m0 0l3 3m-3-3l-3 3M6.75 19.5a4.5 4.5 0
                                 01-1.41-8.775 5.25 5.25 0 0110.233-2.33 3 3 0
                                 013.758 3.848A3.752 3.752 0 0118 19.5H6.75z"/>
                    </svg><span>${i === 0 ? 'Cover' : '+'}</span>`;
                    label.appendChild(empty);

                } else {
                    // Show image + remove button
                    const img = document.createElement('img');
                    img.src = slot.type === 'existing' ? slot.url : URL.createObjectURL(slot.file);
                    img.className = 'ic-image-slot__preview';
                    label.appendChild(img);

                    if (i === 0) {
                        const badge = document.createElement('span');
                        badge.className = 'ic-image-slot__badge';
                        badge.textContent = 'Cover';
                        label.appendChild(badge);
                    }

                    // Prevent the label's file-picker behaviour
                    label.style.cursor = 'default';

                    const removeBtn = document.createElement('button');
                    removeBtn.type = 'button';
                    removeBtn.className = 'ic-image-slot__remove';
                    removeBtn.innerHTML = '&times;';
                    removeBtn.addEventListener('click', e => { e.preventDefault(); removeSlot(i); });
                    label.appendChild(removeBtn);
                }

                imageGrid.appendChild(label);
            });
        }

        async function handleNewImage(slot, file) {
            if (!file) return;
            if (file.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) { showError('errImages', `Image exceeds 5 MB.`); return; }
            showError('errImages', '');

            // Upload immediately
            const fd = new FormData();
            fd.append('itemId', ITEM_ID);
            fd.append('slot', slot);
            fd.append('file', file);
            const res = await postForm(IMG_UPLOAD_URL, fd);

            if (!res.ok) { showError('errImages', res.error); return; }

            imageSlots[slot] = { type: 'existing', url: res.url };
            renderImageGrid();
        }

        async function removeSlot(slot) {
            const s = imageSlots[slot];
            if (s.type === 'existing') {
                const fd = new FormData();
                fd.append('itemId', ITEM_ID);
                fd.append('url', s.url);
                await postForm(IMG_REMOVE_URL, fd);
            }
            imageSlots[slot] = { type: 'empty' };
            renderImageGrid();
        }

        renderImageGrid();

        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  VARIANT BUILDER — pre-populated
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        const variantList   = document.getElementById('variantList');
        const addVariantBtn = document.getElementById('addVariantBtn');
        const skuTemplate   = document.getElementById('skuTemplate');

        function addVariant(existingVariant) {
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'ic-variant-card';

            const vId = existingVariant?.variantId ?? null;
            if (vId) card.dataset.variantId = vId;

            card.innerHTML = `
                <div class="ic-variant-header">
                    <div class="ic-field" style="flex:1">
                        <label class="ic-field__label">Variant Name</label>
                        <input type="text" class="ic-field__input ic-variant__name"
                               value="${existingVariant?.name ?? ''}"
                               placeholder="e.g. Red, Navy, Classic Fit" maxlength="50" />
                        <p class="ic-field__error ic-variant__name-error" hidden></p>
                    </div>
                    <button type="button" class="ic-variant__remove" aria-label="Remove variant">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14">
                            <path d="M11 1.75V3h2.25a.75.75 0 010 1.5H2.75a.75.75 0 010-1.5H5V1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h2.5C10.216 0 11 .784 11 1.75zM4.496 6.675a.75.75 0 10-1.492.15l.66 6.6A1.75 1.75 0 005.405 15h5.19a1.75 1.75 0 001.741-1.575l.66-6.6a.75.75 0 10-1.492-.15l-.66 6.6a.25.25 0 01-.249.225H5.405a.25.25 0 01-.249-.225l-.66-6.6z"/>
                        </svg>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <div class="ic-sku-list">
                    <div class="ic-sku-header">
                        <span>Size</span><span>Price</span><span>Quantity</span><span></span>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <button type="button" class="tl-btn tl-btn--ghost ic-add-sku">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="12" height="12">
                        <path d="M7.75 2a.75.75 0 01.75.75V7h4.25a.75.75 0 010 1.5H8.5v4.25a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0V8.5H2.75a.75.75 0 010-1.5H7V2.75A.75.75 0 017.75 2z"/>
                    </svg>
                    Add Size / SKU
                </button>
                <p class="ic-field__error ic-variant__sku-error" hidden></p>`;

            card.querySelector('.ic-variant__remove').addEventListener('click', () => card.remove());
            card.querySelector('.ic-add-sku').addEventListener('click', () =>
                addSku(card.querySelector('.ic-sku-list'), null));

            variantList.appendChild(card);

            // Pre-populate SKUs
            if (existingVariant?.skus?.length) {
                existingVariant.skus.forEach(s => addSku(card.querySelector('.ic-sku-list'), s));
            } else {
                addSku(card.querySelector('.ic-sku-list'), null);
            }
        }

        function addSku(skuList, existingSku) {
            const row = skuTemplate.content.cloneNode(true).querySelector('.ic-sku-row');
            if (existingSku?.skuId) row.dataset.skuId = existingSku.skuId;

            const sizeSelect = row.querySelector('.ic-sku__size');
            const priceInput = row.querySelector('.ic-sku__price');
            const qtyInput   = row.querySelector('.ic-sku__qty');

            if (existingSku) {
                if (existingSku.size) sizeSelect.value = existingSku.size;
                priceInput.value = existingSku.price;
                qtyInput.value   = existingSku.quantity;
            }

            row.querySelector('.ic-sku__remove').addEventListener('click', () => row.remove());
            skuList.appendChild(row);
        }

        // Pre-populate from server data
        EXISTING_VARIANTS.forEach(v => addVariant(v));
        addVariantBtn.addEventListener('click', () => addVariant(null));

        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  SAVE
        // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        function buildPayload() {
            let valid = true;

            const title     = document.getElementById('itemTitle').value.trim();
            const desc      = document.getElementById('itemDesc').value.trim();
            const category  = document.getElementById('itemCategory').value;
            const condition = document.getElementById('itemCondition').value;

            showError('errTitle', '');
            showError('errDesc', '');
            showError('errCategory', '');
            showError('errCondition', '');
            showError('errVariants', '');
            showGlobal('');

            if (!title)     { showError('errTitle',    'Title is required.');          valid = false; }
            if (!desc)      { showError('errDesc',     'Description is required.');    valid = false; }
            if (!category)  { showError('errCategory', 'Please select a category.');   valid = false; }
            if (!condition) { showError('errCondition','Please select a condition.');   valid = false; }

            const variantCards = variantList.querySelectorAll('.ic-variant-card');
            if (!variantCards.length) { showError('errVariants', 'Add at least one variant.'); valid = false; }

            const variants = [];
            variantCards.forEach(card => {
                const nameInput = card.querySelector('.ic-variant__name');
                const nameErr   = card.querySelector('.ic-variant__name-error');
                const skuErr    = card.querySelector('.ic-variant__sku-error');
                nameErr.hidden = skuErr.hidden = true;

                const name = nameInput.value.trim();
                if (!name) { nameErr.textContent = 'Variant name is required.'; nameErr.hidden = false; valid = false; }

                const skus = [];
                card.querySelectorAll('.ic-sku-row').forEach(row => {
                    const price = parseFloat(row.querySelector('.ic-sku__price').value);
                    const qty   = parseInt(row.querySelector('.ic-sku__qty').value, 10);
                    const size  = row.querySelector('.ic-sku__size').value;

                    if (isNaN(price) || price <= 0) { skuErr.textContent = 'All SKUs need a valid price.'; skuErr.hidden = false; valid = false; return; }
                    if (isNaN(qty)   || qty < 1)    { skuErr.textContent = 'All SKUs need a valid quantity.'; skuErr.hidden = false; valid = false; return; }

                    const skuId = row.dataset.skuId ? parseInt(row.dataset.skuId) : null;
                    skus.push({ skuId, size: size || null, price, quantity: qty });
                });

                if (!skus.length) { skuErr.textContent = 'Add at least one SKU.'; skuErr.hidden = false; valid = false; }

                const variantId = card.dataset.variantId ? parseInt(card.dataset.variantId) : null;
                variants.push({ variantId, name, skus });
            });

            if (!valid) return null;

            return { shopItemId: ITEM_ID, title, description: desc, category, condition, variants };
        }

        document.getElementById('saveBtn').addEventListener('click', async () => {
            const payload = buildPayload();
            if (!payload) return;

            const btn = document.getElementById('saveBtn');
            btn.disabled    = true;
            btn.textContent = 'Saving…';

            const res = await postJson(EDIT_URL, payload);

            btn.disabled    = false;
            btn.textContent = 'Save Changes';

            if (!res.ok) { showGlobal(res.error ?? 'Failed to save changes.'); return; }

            window.location.href = `/Shop/Details/@Model.ItemId`;
        });

    }());
</script>

<style>
    /* Reuses .ic-* classes from Create view — identical design language */
    .ic-shell {
        max-width: 760px;
        margin: 0 auto;
        padding: 1.5rem 1.25rem 4rem;
        display: flex;
        flex-direction: column;
        gap: 1.5rem;
    }

    .ic-header__title {
        font-family: 'DM Serif Display', serif;
        font-size: 1.75rem;
        color: var(--color-text,#1a1814);
        margin: 0.5rem 0 0.25rem;
    }

    .ic-header__sub {
        font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
        font-size: 0.9rem;
        color: var(--color-muted,#8a8278);
        margin: 0;
    }

    .ic-alert {
        display: flex;
        align-items: flex-start;
        gap: 0.5rem;
        border-radius: 8px;
        padding: 0.75rem 1rem;
        font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
        font-size: 0.875rem;
    }

    .ic-alert--error {
        background: color-mix(in srgb, #dc2626 8%, transparent);
        border: 1px solid color-mix(in srgb, #dc2626 20%, transparent);
        color: #b91c1c;
    }

    .ic-card {
        background: #fff;
        border: 1px solid var(--color-border,#e2ddd6);
        border-radius: 14px;
        padding: 1.5rem;
        display: flex;
        flex-direction: column;
        gap: 1.25rem;
    }

    .ic-card__label {
        font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
        font-size: 0.75rem;
        font-weight: 700;
        letter-spacing: 0.07em;
        text-transform: uppercase;
        color: var(--color-muted,#8a8278);
    }

    .ic-card__label-hint {
        font-weight: 400;
        font-size: 0.78rem;
        text-transform: none;
        letter-spacing: 0;
        color: var(--color-muted,#8a8278);
        margin-left: 0.5rem;
    }

    .ic-card__label-hint--block {
        display: block;
        margin: 0.2rem 0 0;
    }

    .ic-card__label-row {
        display: flex;
        align-items: flex-start;
        justify-content: space-between;
        gap: 1rem;
    }

    .ic-grid {
        display: grid;
        grid-template-columns: 1fr 1fr;
        gap: 1.25rem;
    }

    .ic-field--full {
        grid-column: 1 / -1;
    }

    .ic-field {
        display: flex;
        flex-direction: column;
        gap: 0.375rem;
    }

    .ic-field__label {
        font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
        font-size: 0.875rem;
        font-weight: 600;
        color: var(--color-text,#1a1814);
    }

    .ic-field__input, .ic-field__textarea, .ic-field__select {
        padding: 0.75rem 0.875rem;
        border: 1.5px solid var(--color-border,#e2ddd6);
        border-radius: 8px;
        font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
        font-size: 0.9rem;
        color: var(--color-text,#1a1814);
        background: #fff;
        outline: none;
        transition: border-color 0.15s;
        width: 100%;
        box-sizing: border-box;
    }

    .ic-field__textarea {
        resize: vertical;
        min-height: 100px;
    }

        .ic-field__input:focus, .ic-field__textarea:focus, .ic-field__select:focus {
            border-color: var(--color-primary,#2d5a27);
        }

    .ic-field__error {
        font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
        font-size: 0.8rem;
        color: #dc2626;
        margin: 0;
    }

    .ic-images {
        display: grid;
        grid-template-columns: repeat(5, 1fr);
        gap: 0.75rem;
    }

    .ic-image-slot {
        aspect-ratio: 1;
        border: 2px dashed var(--color-border,#e2ddd6);
        border-radius: 10px;
        cursor: pointer;

@if (isOwner)
{
    <input type="hidden" id="afToken" value="@afToken" />

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            const SHOP_ID      = @Model.ShopId;
            const AF_TOKEN     = document.getElementById('afToken').value;
            const FIELD_URL    = '/Shop/SaveField';
            const IMAGE_URL    = '/Shop/SaveImage';

            // ── AJAX: text field ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
            async function saveTextField(field, value) {
                const res = await fetch(FIELD_URL, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                        'RequestVerificationToken': AF_TOKEN
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ shopId: SHOP_ID, field, value })
                });
                return res.json();
            }

            // ── AJAX: image upload ───────────────────────────────────────────────
            async function uploadImage(field, file) {
                const fd = new FormData();
                fd.append('shopId', SHOP_ID);
                fd.append('field',  field);
                fd.append('file',   file);

                const res = await fetch(IMAGE_URL, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'RequestVerificationToken': AF_TOKEN },
                    body: fd
                });
                return res.json();
            }

            // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
            //  IMAGE MODAL
            // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
            const backdrop    = document.getElementById('imgModalBackdrop');
            const modalTitle  = document.getElementById('imgModalTitle');
            const previewArea = document.getElementById('imgPreviewArea');
            const dropZone    = document.getElementById('imgDropZone');
            const fileInput   = document.getElementById('imgFileInput');
            const dropInner   = document.getElementById('imgDropInner');
            const saveBtn     = document.getElementById('imgModalSave');
            const cancelBtn   = document.getElementById('imgModalCancel');
            const closeBtn    = document.getElementById('imgModalClose');
            const errorEl     = document.getElementById('imgModalError');

            let activeField   = null;
            let pendingFile   = null;

            // ── Open modal ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            function openModal(field, currentUrl, title) {
                activeField  = field;
                pendingFile  = null;
                saveBtn.disabled = true;
                errorEl.hidden   = true;
                fileInput.value  = '';
                modalTitle.textContent = title;

                // Show current image as preview if one exists
                previewArea.innerHTML = '';
                if (currentUrl) {
                    if (field === 'BannerUrl') {
                        const div = document.createElement('div');
                        div.className = 'sp-modal__banner-preview';
                        div.style.backgroundImage = `url('${currentUrl}')`;
                        previewArea.appendChild(div);
                    } else {
                        const img = document.createElement('img');
                        img.src = currentUrl;
                        img.className = 'sp-modal__logo-preview';
                        previewArea.appendChild(img);
                    }
                } else {
                    const empty = document.createElement('div');
                    empty.className = 'sp-modal__preview-empty';
                    empty.textContent = 'No image set';
                    previewArea.appendChild(empty);
                }

                // Reset drop zone label
                dropInner.querySelector('.sp-modal__drop-label').textContent =
                    'Click or drag an image here';

                backdrop.removeAttribute('hidden');
                dropZone.focus();
            }

            function closeModal() {
                backdrop.setAttribute('hidden', '');
                activeField  = null;
                pendingFile  = null;
            }

            closeBtn?.addEventListener('click',  closeModal);
            cancelBtn?.addEventListener('click', closeModal);
            backdrop?.addEventListener('click',  e => { if (e.target === backdrop) closeModal(); });
            document.addEventListener('keydown', e => { if (e.key === 'Escape') closeModal(); });

            // ── File selection (click or drag) ───────────────────────────────────
            function handleFile(file) {
                if (!file) return;

                const allowed = ['image/jpeg','image/png','image/webp','image/gif'];
                if (!allowed.includes(file.type)) {
                    showModalError('Only JPEG, PNG, WebP, or GIF images are allowed.');
                    return;
                }
                if (file.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) {
                    showModalError('File exceeds the 5 MB limit.');
                    return;
                }

                errorEl.hidden = true;
                pendingFile    = file;
                saveBtn.disabled = false;

                // Live preview using FileReader
                const reader = new FileReader();
                reader.onload = e => {
                    previewArea.innerHTML = '';
                    if (activeField === 'BannerUrl') {
                        const div = document.createElement('div');
                        div.className = 'sp-modal__banner-preview';
                        div.style.backgroundImage = `url('${e.target.result}')`;
                        previewArea.appendChild(div);
                    } else {
                        const img = document.createElement('img');
                        img.src = e.target.result;
                        img.className = 'sp-modal__logo-preview';
                        previewArea.appendChild(img);
                    }
                };
                reader.readAsDataURL(file);

                dropInner.querySelector('.sp-modal__drop-label').textContent = file.name;
            }

            fileInput?.addEventListener('change', () => handleFile(fileInput.files[0]));

            // Drag-and-drop
            dropZone?.addEventListener('dragover',  e => { e.preventDefault(); dropZone.classList.add('sp-modal__drop-zone--over'); });
            dropZone?.addEventListener('dragleave', ()  => dropZone.classList.remove('sp-modal__drop-zone--over'));
            dropZone?.addEventListener('drop', e => {
                e.preventDefault();
                dropZone.classList.remove('sp-modal__drop-zone--over');
                handleFile(e.dataTransfer.files[0]);
            });

            // ── Upload ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            saveBtn?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
                if (!pendingFile || !activeField) return;

                saveBtn.disabled     = true;
                saveBtn.textContent  = 'Uploading…';
                errorEl.hidden       = true;

                const res = await uploadImage(activeField, pendingFile);

                saveBtn.disabled    = false;
                saveBtn.textContent = 'Upload';

                if (!res.ok) {
                    showModalError(res.error);
                    return;
                }

                // Update the page live without a reload
                const cacheBuster = `${res.url}?v=${Date.now()}`;

                if (activeField === 'BannerUrl') {
                    const banner = document.getElementById('shopBanner');
                    banner.style.backgroundImage = `url('${cacheBuster}')`;
                    banner.querySelector('.sp-banner__placeholder')?.remove();
                } else {
                    const wrap     = document.getElementById('shopLogoWrap');
                    const existing = document.getElementById('shopLogoImg');
                    if (existing.tagName === 'DIV') {
                        // Replace the initial letter placeholder with an actual img
                        const img  = document.createElement('img');
                        img.src    = cacheBuster;
                        img.id     = 'shopLogoImg';
                        img.alt    = 'Shop logo';
                        img.className = 'sp-identity__logo';
                        existing.replaceWith(img);
                    } else {
                        existing.src = cacheBuster;
                    }
                }

                closeModal();
            });

            function showModalError(msg) {
                errorEl.textContent = msg;
                errorEl.hidden      = false;
            }

            // ── Banner click ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            document.getElementById('shopBanner')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
                const raw     = document.getElementById('shopBanner').style.backgroundImage;
                const current = raw ? raw.replace(/^url\(['"]?/,'').replace(/['"]?\)$/,'') : null;
                openModal('BannerUrl', current || null, 'Banner Image');
            });

            // ── Logo click ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            const logoWrap = document.getElementById('shopLogoWrap');
            if (logoWrap) {
                const openLogo = () => {
                    const img     = document.getElementById('shopLogoImg');
                    const current = img?.tagName === 'IMG' ? img.src : null;
                    openModal('LogoUrl', current, 'Logo Image');
                };
                logoWrap.addEventListener('click', openLogo);
                logoWrap.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
                    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') { e.preventDefault(); openLogo(); }
                });
            }

            // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
            //  INLINE TEXT EDITING (ShopName + Bio)
            // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
            document.querySelectorAll('.sp-inline--editable').forEach(block => {
                const display   = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__display');
                const editor    = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__editor');
                const input     = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__input');
                const saveBtn   = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__save');
                const cancelBtn = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__cancel');
                const errorEl   = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__error');
                const field     = block.dataset.field;

                if (!display || !editor || !input) return;

                let originalValue = input.value;

                function openEditor() {
                    input.value = originalValue;
                    display.hidden = true;
                    editor.removeAttribute('hidden');
                    block.classList.add('sp-inline--editing');
                    input.focus();
                    if (input.tagName === 'INPUT')
                        input.setSelectionRange(input.value.length, input.value.length);
                }

                function closeEditor(restore) {
                    if (restore) input.value = originalValue;
                    display.hidden = false;
                    editor.setAttribute('hidden', '');
                    errorEl.hidden = true;
                    block.classList.remove('sp-inline--editing');
                }

                display.addEventListener('click', openEditor);
                cancelBtn.addEventListener('click', () => closeEditor(true));

                input.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
                    if (e.key === 'Escape') { e.preventDefault(); closeEditor(true); }
                    if ((e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey) && e.key === 'Enter') saveBtn.click();
                });

                saveBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
                    const val = input.value.trim();
                    errorEl.hidden      = true;
                    saveBtn.disabled    = true;
                    saveBtn.textContent = 'Saving…';

                    const res = await saveTextField(field, val);

                    saveBtn.disabled    = false;
                    saveBtn.textContent = 'Save';

                    if (!res.ok) {
                        errorEl.textContent = res.error;
                        errorEl.hidden      = false;
                        return;
                    }

                    originalValue = val;

                    if (field === 'ShopName') {
                        display.textContent = val;
                        document.title = val;
                    } else {
                        display.textContent = val || 'Click to add a bio...';
                        display.classList.toggle('sp-identity__bio--empty', !val);
                    }

                    closeEditor(false);
                });
            });

        }());
    </script>
}

            opacity: 0.65;

    </style>

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var input   = document.getElementById('amountInput');
            var form    = document.getElementById('addFundsForm');
            var btn     = document.getElementById('addFundsBtn');
            var presets = document.querySelectorAll('.addfunds-quick__btn');

            presets.forEach(function (p) {
                p.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    if (!input) return;
                    input.value = p.dataset.amount;
                    presets.forEach(function (b) { b.classList.remove('addfunds-quick__btn--active'); });
                    p.classList.add('addfunds-quick__btn--active');
                });
            });

            if (input) {
                input.addEventListener('input', function () {
                    presets.forEach(function (b) { b.classList.remove('addfunds-quick__btn--active'); });
                    presets.forEach(function (b) {
                        if (b.dataset.amount === input.value) b.classList.add('addfunds-quick__btn--active');
                    });
                });
            }

            if (form && btn) {
                form.addEventListener('submit', function () {
                    btn.disabled = true;
                    btn.textContent = 'Processing…';
                });
            }
        }());
    </script>
}

    <script>
        (function () {

            var amountInput = document.getElementById('amountInput');
            var allBtn      = document.getElementById('withdrawAllBtn');
            var wdForm      = document.getElementById('wdForm');
            var wdSubmitBtn = document.getElementById('wdSubmitBtn');
            var methodRadios = document.querySelectorAll('.wd-method-radio');
            var methodLabels = document.querySelectorAll('.wd-method-option');

            // "Withdraw all" shortcut
            if (allBtn && amountInput) {
                allBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    amountInput.value = amountInput.max;
                });
            }

            // Sync method option visual state with radio selection
            methodRadios.forEach(function (radio, i) {
                radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                    methodLabels.forEach(function (lbl) { lbl.classList.remove('wd-method-option--active'); });
                    if (radio.checked) methodLabels[i].classList.add('wd-method-option--active');
                });
            });

            // Update reference hint based on method
            var referenceHint = document.getElementById('referenceHint');
            methodRadios.forEach(function (radio) {
                radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                    if (!referenceHint) return;
                    referenceHint.textContent = radio.value === '1'
                        ? 'Your preferred pickup location or reference code.'
                        : 'Your bank account number or preferred pickup reference.';
                });
            });

            // Disable submit while in-flight
            if (wdForm && wdSubmitBtn) {
                wdForm.addEventListener('submit', function () {
                    wdSubmitBtn.disabled = true;
                    wdSubmitBtn.textContent = 'Submitting…';
                });
            }
        }());
    </script>
}
